    carrier_story: CFP-1336
    date: 2026-05-24

# ADR-082: Write-time self-write verification mandate вҖ” internal lane agent В§9 evidence / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration verify super-class

## мғҒнғң

Accepted (2026-05-17 KST) вҖ” CFP-776 carrier. PMOAgent ADR-045 В§D-9 cross_story_pattern_adr_trigger pattern_count 3 вүҘ threshold 2 мӮ°л¬ј (escalation_action `escalate_user` вҶ’ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӢЁмқј super-class ADR нҶөн•© кІ°м • 2026-05-16 KST). doc-only fast-path (ADR-054 лӢЁмқј PR).

## ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё

lane agent (RequirementsPL / ArchitectAgent / DeveloperPL л“ұ) к°Җ В§9 evidence мһ‘м„ұ / Phase 0 ChangeImpactAgent mapping / Story corpus enumeration мӢң **write-time м—җ source/value/ownership мқ„ verify м—Ҷмқҙ лӢЁм–ё**н•ҳлҠ” кІғмқ„ кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ. мһ‘м„ұн•ң **к°’ мһҗмІҙк°Җ мӮ¬мӢӨкіј мқјм№ҳн•ҳлҠ”к°Җ** лҘј write м§Ғм „ source direct verify нӣ„ write н•ңлӢӨ. ліё ADR мқҙ м¶©мЎұлҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©ҙ м•„лһҳ В§кІ°м • mechanism мқ„ лӘҮ к°ң мҢ“л“  мқҳлҜё м—ҶлӢӨ вҖ” лӘЁл“  В§кІ°м • мқҖ ліём§Ҳмқ„ ліҙмЎ°н•ҳлҠ” scaffolding.

кё°мЎҙ codeforge governance мқҳ self-write кІҖмҰқ layer лҠ” (1) **write к¶Ңн•ң actor кІҪкі„** (`measurement-channel.md` вҖ” ledger write = Orchestrator monopoly) + (2) **syntactic ownership** (`lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.md` INV-DI-1/2 вҖ” non-owner destructive write / monopoly unauthorized mutation) л§Ң м •мқҳн•ңлӢӨ. **(3) write-time semantic truth (мһ‘м„ұ к°’мқҙ мӮ¬мӢӨкіј мқјм№ҳн•ҳлҠ”к°Җ) verify layer = лӘ…л°ұн•ң лҸ„л©”мқё кіөл°ұ** (verified-via: `git show origin/main:docs/domain-knowledge/domain/governance-principle/lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.md` + `git show origin/main:docs/domain-knowledge/domain/orchestrator-discipline/measurement-channel.md`, DomainAgent Phase 0 Read вҖ” "write-time" / "semantic truth" нӮӨмӣҢл“ң 0кұҙ л§Өм№ӯ). ADR-082 к°Җ мқҙ (3) layer мӢ м„Ө anchor.

## м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

### pattern corpus (3 лҲ„м Ғ вҖ” Issue #776 body verbatim)

| # | Story | л°ңнҳ„ | м„ӨлӘ… |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1a | CFP-746 | D-7 м„Өкі„ corpus slip | мқҙм „ м„Өкі„ pass к°Җ "corpus м—җ same-repo `story_issues[]` мҳҲмӢң м „л¬ҙ" лӢЁм • вҶ’ мӢӨм ң CFP-275/280/281/282/283 5кұҙ same-repo ліҙмң . factually FALSE corpus лӢЁм • (ADR-052 TP#2 P1-2 м Ғл°ң, ADR-070 Orchestrator verify нҷ•м •) |
| 1b | CFP-746 | CFP-531 м •м •-2nd-slip | D-7 м •м •мқҙ CFP-531 мқ„ same-repo fixture 6лІҲм§ё м¶”к°Җ вҶ’ мӢӨм ң CFP-531 frontmatter cross-repo (`github_issue:` only, `story_issues:` block л¶Җмһ¬). **м •м • н–үмң„ мһҗмІҙ лҜёкІҖмҰқ** вҶ’ 2nd unverified-corpus-claim лҸ„мһ… (ADR-052 TP#2 re-check RESIDUAL P2 м Ғл°ң) |
| 2 | CFP-770 | CR-004 В§9 evidence stale | В§9 write мӢң ADR-079 frontmatter `is_transitional: true` + н•ҙмҶҢкё°мӨҖ 3-tuple кё°мһ¬ вҶ’ мӢӨм ң ADR-079:7 `is_transitional: false` / N/A permanent policy. В§9 evidence мһҗмІҙк°Җ source verify м—Ҷмқҙ value лӢЁм–ё |
| 3 | CFP-770 | В§кІ°м • 8 Phase 0 cross-plugin м¶”м • | spec/Story В§4.0 мҙҲм•Ҳмқҙ "5 template м „л¶Җ wrapper-local" к°Җм • вҶ’ мӢӨм ң wrapper 2 + cross-plugin 3 (codeforge-design `adr.md`/`change-plan.md`, codeforge-pmo `retro.md`). ChangeImpactAgent Phase 0 mapping cross-plugin ownership лҜёкІҖмҰқ |

PMOAgent ADR-045 Amendment 5 В§D-9 м •лҹү мһ„кі„к°’: pattern_count **3** вүҘ threshold 2 вҶ’ Mandatory framing + escalation_action `escalate_user` вҶ’ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӢЁмқј super-class ADR нҶөн•© кІ°м •.

### нҳ„ SSOT кІ°кІ© мҳҒм—ӯ

- **ADR-073** = Orchestrator к°Җ cross-repo state / assumption лӢЁм • мӢң verify + annotation мқҳл¬ҙ вҶ’ *Orchestrator н–үмң„* н•ңм • (internal lane self-write лҜёнҸ¬н•Ё, verified-via: `git show origin/main:docs/adr/ADR-073...md` title="cross-repo ground truth + assumption verify mandate" 2026-05-17 KST).
- **ADR-070** = Codex external worker output verify мқҳл¬ҙ вҶ’ *мҷёл¶Җ worker(Codex) output* н•ңм • (verified-via: `git show origin/main:docs/adr/ADR-070...md` title="Codex verify-before-trust pattern (sandbox access invariant)" 2026-05-17 KST).
- **ліё super-class gap** = lane agent к°Җ В§9 evidence мһ‘м„ұ / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration мӢң **write-time** м—җ source/value/ownership мқ„ verify м—Ҷмқҙ лӢЁм–ён•ҳлҠ” мҳҒм—ӯ вҖ” м„Өкі„ lane, В§9 write, Phase 0 agent лӘЁл‘җ ADR-073/070 scope мҷё.

## кІ°м •

### В§кІ°м • 1 вҖ” Layer disjoint нҢҗм • н‘ң (мқҳл¬ҙ вҖ” PMOAgent мң„н—ҳ мҷ„нҷ”)

verify-before-trust governance лҠ” 4 disjoint layer лЎң кө¬м„ұлҗңлӢӨ. к°Ғ layer лҠ” verify лҢҖмғҒ / н–үмң„ мЈјмІҙк°Җ м„ңлЎң disjoint н•ҳл©°, ліё н‘ңк°Җ 4-layer мқҳ кіөнҶө anchor лӢӨ.

| Layer | ADR | verify лҢҖмғҒ / scope |
|---|---|---|
| Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify | ADR-073 | Orchestrator н–үмң„ н•ңм • вҖ” cross-repo state + assumption кё°мҲ  мӢң `git fetch` + `git show origin/main:<path>` direct verify + `verified-via` annotation |
| external worker (Codex) output verify | ADR-070 | мҷёл¶Җ worker output н•ңм • вҖ” Codex finding evidence ground truth лҘј Orchestrator direct file Read лЎң verify, mismatch мӢң verdict reject |
| **internal lane agent self-write verify (ліё ADR)** | **ADR-082** | **lane agent В§9 evidence / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration write-time** вҖ” мһ‘м„ұ к°’ мһҗмІҙк°Җ мӮ¬мӢӨкіј мқјм№ҳн•ҳлҠ”к°Җ source direct verify нӣ„ write |
| retro corpus enumeration (PMOAgent В§5 pattern_count) | ADR-045 В§D | retro pattern aggregation вҖ” cross-Story pattern_count вүҘ threshold кІҖм¶ң мӢң ADR escalation forcing function |

> **4-layer м¶©л¶„ (5th row л¶Ҳмҡ”)**: ADR-078 (CFP-756 design doc lifecycle living design doc) лҠ” verify-before-trust мҷҖ лі„ axis (мҳҒмҶҚ кө¬мЎ° л¬ём„ң lifecycle вү  write-time semantic truth) мқҙл©° origin/main лҜёмЎҙмһ¬ (verified-via: `git ls-tree origin/main docs/adr/` вҶ’ ADR-078 file л¶Җмһ¬ 2026-05-17 KST). 5th row м¶”к°Җ л¶Ҳмҡ”.

### В§кІ°м • 2 вҖ” Write-time verify мқҳл¬ҙ (scope a-d)

lane agent к°Җ owned section м—җ м•„лһҳ 4 мў… write лҘј мҲҳн–үн•  л•Ң write м§Ғм „ source direct verify нӣ„ write н•ңлӢӨ.

- **(a) corpus / fixture enumeration** вҖ” Story / Change-Plan / ADR ліёл¬ём—җ "мҳҲмӢң Nкұҙ / м „л¬ҙ / л¶Җмһ¬ / лӢӨмҲҳ" + file-path мқёмҡ© нҢЁн„ҙмқ„ write н•  л•Ң вҶ’ `git show origin/main:<path>` verify нӣ„ `[verified: git show origin/main:<path>]` annotation л¶Җм°© мқҳл¬ҙ. annotation л¶Җмһ¬ = behavioral violation. (ADR-068 I-5 dimensional empirical-source annotation кіј **directly analogous mechanical нҢЁн„ҙ** вҖ” лҸҷмқј mechanical нҢЁн„ҙ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳлӮҳ, ліё ADR мқҖ В§кІ°м • 6 known-limitation мңјлЎң behavioral mandate only. mechanical lint лҠ” нӣ„мҶҚ carrier.) вҖ” corpus #1a (CFP-746 D-7) м°ЁлӢЁ.
- **(b) design-lane self-check** вҖ” ArchitectAgent В§3 / В§7 corpus enumeration + ADR frontmatter value мқёмҡ© мӢң `git show origin/main` мңјлЎң verify нӣ„ write. **м •м • н–үмң„ мһҗмІҙлҸ„ лҸҷмқј verify мқҳл¬ҙ** (м •м •мқҙ лҜёкІҖмҰқлҗҳм–ҙ 2nd slip мқ„ лҸ„мһ…н•ң corpus #1b CFP-531 лҸҷмқё вҖ” В§кІ°м • 3 мһ¬к·Җ cross-ref). вҖ” corpus #1b м°ЁлӢЁ.
- **(c) В§9 evidence write-time verify** вҖ” lane agent к°Җ В§9 verdict evidence м—җ ADR frontmatter value / contract field value лҘј кё°мһ¬н•  л•Ң вҶ’ source file direct Read verify нӣ„ write. (corpus #2 CFP-770 CR-004 лҸҷмқё вҖ” В§9 write мӢң ADR-079 `is_transitional` value лҘј source verify м—Ҷмқҙ stale лӢЁм–ё.) вҖ” corpus #2 м°ЁлӢЁ.
- **(d) Phase 0 cross-plugin ownership verify** вҖ” ChangeImpactAgent Phase 0 mapping мӢң `templates/*` н•ӯлӘ©мқ„ wrapper-local лӢЁм •н•ҳкё° м „ cross-plugin SSOT verify 1-step мқҳл¬ҙ. verify source = `codeforge:lane-self-write-boundary` skill. (corpus #3 CFP-770 В§кІ°м • 8 лҸҷмқё + memory `project_stale_skill_ownership_lore` 2nd мһ¬нҳ„ вҖ” cross-plugin ownership м¶”м •.) **known-limitation: verify source к°Җ mechanical-queryable registry нҳ•нғң л¶Җмһ¬ вҖ” В§кІ°м • 6 rationale binding м°ёмЎ°.** вҖ” corpus #3 м°ЁлӢЁ.

### В§кІ°м • 3 вҖ” м •м • н–үмң„ мһ¬к·Җ verify + л¬ҙн•ң лЈЁн”„ cap (Researcher Unknown #1)

В§кІ°м • 2 verify лҲ„лқҪмқҙ мӮ¬нӣ„ м •м •лҗ  л•Ң, **м •м • write лҸ„ мғҲ self-write artifact мқҙлҜҖлЎң лҸҷмқј В§кІ°м • 2 verify лҢҖмғҒ** (мһ¬к·Җ). corpus #1b (CFP-746 CFP-531) к°Җ "м •м •мқҙ лҜёкІҖмҰқлҗҳм–ҙ 2nd slip лҸ„мһ…" мқҳ мӢӨмҰқ evidence.

мһ¬к·Җ м •м • (verify the fix of the verify, of the verify, вҖҰ) л¬ҙн•ң лЈЁн”„ м°ЁлӢЁ = **мӢ к·ң л¬ҙн•ңлЈЁн”„ м°ЁлӢЁ л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ лҜёлҸ„мһ…, кё°мЎҙ layer мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©**: ADR-067 кІ°м • 1 (max FIX 3/3 лҸ„лӢ¬ мӢң deterministic implementability reassessment trigger) + кІ°м • 3 (ArchitectPL мһ¬лҹү RESET vs escalation кІ°м • к¶Ңн•ң) ліөн•© cross-ref. м •м • мһ¬к·Җк°Җ max FIX 3/3 лҸ„лӢ¬ мӢң ADR-067 кІ°м • 1 reassessment trigger л°ңлҸҷ вҶ’ кІ°м • 3 ArchitectPL мһ¬лҹүмңјлЎң RESET vs `escalate_to_user` кІ°м • (ADR-067 кІ°м • 2 escalation мқҳл¬ҙ trigger 3мў… нҸүк°Җ лҸҷл°ҳ). лҸ„л©”мқёмғҒ мқҙлҜё мЎҙмһ¬н•ҳлҠ” л¬ҙн•ңлЈЁн”„ м°ЁлӢЁ л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳмқ„ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© (over-engineering нҡҢн”ј).

### В§кІ°м • 4 вҖ” Citation вү  Assertion кІҪкі„ (Analyst E-1)

lane agent owned section лӮҙ cross-lane мӮ°м¶ңл¬јм—җ лҢҖн•ң **мқёмҡ©(citation, м¶ңмІҳ лӘ…мӢң)** кіј **лӢЁм •(assertion, к°’мқ„ мӮ¬мӢӨлЎң мЈјмһҘ)** мқҖ лҸ„л©”мқёмғҒ лӢӨлҘё н–үмң„лӢӨ.

- **citation** = м¶ңмІҳ attribution мңјлЎң м¶©л¶„ (мҳҲ: "RequirementsPL В§5 к°Җ doc-only м ҒкІ©мңјлЎң нҢҗм •" вҖ” м¶ңмІҳ лӘ…мӢң) вҶ’ verify л©ҙм ң.
- **assertion** = к°’мқ„ мӮ¬мӢӨлЎң мЈјмһҘ (мҳҲ: "ADR-079 frontmatter `is_transitional: false`" вҖ” к°’ лӢЁм–ё) вҶ’ В§кІ°м • 2 verify мқҳл¬ҙ.

В§кІ°м • 2 мқҳ verify мқҳл¬ҙлҠ” **assertion м—җл§Ң** м Ғмҡ©лҗңлӢӨ. cross-lane мӮ°м¶ңл¬јмқ„ м¶ңмІҳмҷҖ н•Ёк»ҳ мқёмҡ©н•ҳлҠ” н–үмң„лҠ” verify мқҳл¬ҙ л°– (verify лҢҖмғҒ = лӢЁм–ёлҗң к°’мқҳ мӮ¬мӢӨм„ұ, мқёмҡ©лҗң нғҖ lane нҢҗм •мқҳ мһ¬кІҖмҰқ м•„лӢҳ).

### В§кІ°м • 5 вҖ” Provisional marker defer (Analyst E-2)

Phase 0 mapping мқҙ planning-phase м§„н–ү мӨ‘ (spec/plan лҜёмҷ„м„ұ) мқј л•ҢлҠ” лҜёмҷ„м„ұ mapping к°’м—җ `[provisional]` marker лҘј л¶Җм°©н•ҳкі  write-time verify лҘј **defer** н•ңлӢӨ. мөңмў… verify мқҳл¬ҙ мӢңм җ = lane spawn м§Ғм „ (`codeforge:story-epic-flow-preflight` preflight лӢЁкі„). planning-phase мҙҲм•Ҳ лӢЁкі„мқҳ verify к°•м ңлҠ” л©ҙм ң (planning л°ҳліө cost нҡҢн”ј) вҖ” лӢЁ `[provisional]` marker л¶Җмһ¬ мӢң В§кІ°м • 2 к°Җ мҰүмӢң м Ғмҡ© (defer л©ҙм ң мЎ°кұҙ = explicit marker).

### В§кІ°м • 6 вҖ” known-limitation (`mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` empty rationale binding)

ліё ADR frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` к°Җ empty мқё кІғмқҖ **лҲ„лқҪмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј лӘ…мӢңм Ғ known-limitation кІ°м •**мқҙлӢӨ. ADR-040 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 7.A schema м •н•© вҖ” DesignReview lane мқҙ ліё ADR мқ„ "missing `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]`" лЎң flag н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ В§кІ°м • ліёл¬ём—җ explicit binding н•ңлӢӨ.

**rationale** (Wave 1 кІ°м • вҖ” Amendment 1 к°ұмӢ  н‘ңмӢң нҸ¬н•Ё):

1. ~~В§кІ°м • 2(d) verify source = `codeforge:lane-self-write-boundary` skill мқҙ cross-plugin ownership мқҳ verify source мқҙлӮҳ **mechanical-queryable registry нҳ•нғң л¶Җмһ¬**~~ вҶ’ **Amendment 1 (CFP-841) partial-stale м •м •**: Wave 1 мқҳ "mechanical-queryable registry нҳ•нғң л¶Җмһ¬" м „м ңлҠ” partially stale. `docs/domain-knowledge/domain/governance-principle/lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.yaml` machine_readable_ssot к°Җ CFP-722 В§13.A лЎң **мқҙлҜё мӢӨмһ¬** (verified-via: `git show origin/main:skills/lane-self-write-boundary/SKILL.md` L36 machine_readable_ssot + `git show origin/main:docs/domain-knowledge/domain/governance-principle/lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.yaml` sections 1-12). лӢЁ yaml = Story file per-section ownership н•ңм • вҖ” ADR/Change Plan/Retro/domain-knowledge cross-plugin doc owner sub-tree л¶Җмһ¬. вҶ’ scope 2(d) = **мӢ к·ң registry м°Ҫм„Ө м•„лӢҢ кё°мЎҙ yaml мқҳ cross-plugin doc-ownership мҳҒм—ӯ нҷ•мһҘ** (disjoint sub-tree append-only) + lint binding + SKILL.md В§13.B 4-way drift-sync н•ҙмҶҢ (Amendment 1 В§scope 2(d) carrier).
2. В§кІ°м • 2(a) corpus annotation мқҖ ADR-068 I-5 мҷҖ directly analogous mechanical нҢЁн„ҙмқҙлӮҳ, ліё super-class кІ°н•ЁмқҖ (a)/(b)/(c)/(d) 4 scope к°Җ лӢЁмқј anchor лЎң л¬¶мқё unitary scope (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1) вҖ” scope (a) л§Ң л¶Җл¶„ mechanical нҷ” мӢң super-class anchor л¶„м Ҳ. behavioral mandate к°Җ 4 scope кіөнҶө forcing function мңјлЎң мҡ°м„ . **Amendment 1 (CFP-841) м •н•© мң м§Җ**: scope (a) + scope (d) **лҸҷмӢң** mechanical м „нҷҳмңјлЎң anchor л¶„м Ҳ нҡҢн”ј (лӢЁмқј carrier вҖ” scope л¶„лҰ¬ лҜён—Ҳмҡ©). scope 2(b)/2(c) = behavioral mandate мҳҒм—ӯ мң м§Җ (super-class anchor мқҳ behavioral forcing function ліҙмЎҙ).
3. лҸҷмқј нҢЁн„ҙ м„ лЎҖ = ADR-070 В§D5 declaration-only retain (Codex verify-before-trust = behavioral mandate, evidence-checks-registry entry append л©ҙм ң) + ADR-RESERVATION row 81 CFP-819 (`mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` declaration-only, verified-via: `git show origin/main:docs/adr/ADR-RESERVATION.md` row 81 2026-05-17 KST). ADR-073 frontmatter мһҗмІҙлҸ„ Wave 1 = `[]` empty (behavioral directive only) м„ лЎҖ. **Amendment 1 (CFP-841) нӣ„ ліё ADR frontmatter = 2-entry deferred-followup** (Wave 2 вҖ” ADR-040 Amendment 3 self-application Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 progression chain м •н•©).

**нӣ„мҶҚ carrier л°ңмқҳ мқҳл¬ҙ вҖ” Amendment 1 (CFP-841) м¶©мЎұ**: ~~scope (d) verify source мқҳ mechanical-queryable registry нҷ” (cross-plugin ownership registry + lint) = лі„лҸ„ нӣ„мҶҚ CFP carrier л¶„лҰ¬ л°ңмқҳ (escalation_action `escalate_user`, CFP-776 merge нӣ„ л°ңмқҳ к¶ҢмһҘ). scope (a) corpus annotation mechanical lint (ADR-068 I-5 нҢЁн„ҙ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©) = лҸҷмқј нӣ„мҶҚ carrier лҳҗлҠ” лі„лҸ„ CFP л¶„лҰ¬ вҖ” brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •.~~ вҶ’ **CFP-841 лӢЁмқј нҶөн•© carrier лЎң м¶©мЎұ** (brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м • = scope (a) + scope (d) лӢЁмқј carrier, ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1 unitary scope). ліё В§кІ°м • 6 = Wave 1 behavioral mandate + Wave 2 (Amendment 1) deferred-followup mechanical declaration. actual lint script + workflow wire = CFP-841 Phase 2 carrier (Change Plan В§3 SSOT).

**self-referential trap нҡҢн”ј (EC-3 self-protection)**: ADR-082 мһҗмІҙк°Җ corpus #1a/#1b/#2/#3 (CFP-746 D-7 corpus slip / CFP-531 м •м •-2nd-slip / CFP-770 CR-004 `is_transitional` кұ°м§“ лӢЁм–ё / В§кІ°м • 8 Phase 0 cross-plugin м¶”м •) нҢЁн„ҙмқ„ ліёл¬ём—җ мқёмҡ©/нҸ¬н•Ён•ңлӢӨ. ADR-082 frontmatter `is_transitional: false` + `## н•ҙмҶҢ кё°мӨҖ` = `N/A (permanent)` м„ м–ёмқҖ В§кІ°м • 2 verify лҢҖмғҒмқҙ *м•„лӢҲлӢӨ* (ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 м•Ҫнҷ” л°©н–Ҙ л°ңмқҳ м°ЁлӢЁ logic нҶөкіј = permanent м •мұ… м„ м–ё, source verify к°Җ м Ғмҡ©лҗ  mutable value м•„лӢҳ). ліё self-referential л©ҙм ңк°Җ В§кІ°м • ліёл¬ём—җ лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”лҗң self-protection вҖ” DesignReview к°Җ "ADR-082 к°Җ мһҗкё° frontmatter лҘј verify м•Ҳ н–ҲлӢӨ" лЎң flag н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ. **Amendment 1 (CFP-841) нҷ•мһҘ**: scope 2(a) corpus annotation lint мқҳ 4лІҲм§ё FP-мҷ„нҷ” guard (self-referential exemption) к°Җ ліё EC-3 лҘј verbatim мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© вҖ” ADR-082 ліёл¬ё / CFP-776 Story / CFP-841 StoryВ·Change Plan мқҳ corpus #1a/#1b/#2/#3 нҢЁн„ҙ мқёмҡ©мқҖ lint self-flag м°ЁлӢЁ (file allowlist м •н•©, Change Plan В§3.1 guard 4).

### В§кІ°м • 7 вҖ” scope (e) FIX лӘ…м„ё depth-aware л¶„лҰ¬ (scope мҷё)

scope (e) FIX лӘ…м„ё depth-aware scope н•„л“ң (CFP-770 В§8 м ңм•Ҳ вҖ” broken-link/path м •м • FIX лӘ…м„ё мӢң directory depth + м •м • к·ңм№ҷ лІ”мң„ мқҳл¬ҙ н•„л“ң) лҠ” **ліё ADR scope мҷё (лі„лҸ„ CFP л¶„лҰ¬)**. super-class write-time verify mandate (a-d) вҶ” FIX лӘ…м„ё depth-aware (e) = disjoint кҙҖмӢ¬мӮ¬ вҖ” м „мһҗ = write-time truth verify (behavioral) / нӣ„мһҗ = fix-event-v1 schema н•„л“ң нҷ•мһҘ (ADR-008 contract bump + ADR-010 sibling sync лҸҷл°ҳ = мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ). лҸҷмқј Story л¬¶мқҢ мӢң CFP-scope-unitary (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1) мң„л°ҳ. (e) = CFP-770 В§8 reservation Issue carrier (escalation_action `escalate_user`, CFP-776 merge нӣ„ л°ңмқҳ к¶ҢмһҘ).

### В§кІ°м • 8 вҖ” per-area л¶„н•  (scope a/b/c/d к°Ғ лі„ ADR) кұ°л¶Җ (scope мҷё)

4 scope = лӢЁмқј super-class кІ°н•Ёмқҳ 4 layer н‘ңнҳ„. В§кІ°м • 1 layer disjoint н‘ңк°Җ кіөнҶө anchor. ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1 м •н•© вҖ” лӢЁмқј super-class = unitary scope (мҳҒм—ӯлі„ л¶„н•  м•„лӢҳ). per-area л¶„н•  мӢң super-class anchor к°Җ 4 ADR лЎң л¶„м Ҳлҗҳм–ҙ cross-Story pattern aggregation (ADR-045 В§D-9) мқҳ forcing function м•Ҫнҷ”.

### В§кІ°м • 9 вҖ” Amendment лІҲнҳё citation plan-time staleness м°ЁлӢЁ (Amendment 6 мӢ м„Ө, CFP-1198 вҖ” Amendment 7 м–‘л°©н–Ҙ нҷ•мһҘ, CFP-1312)

**forcing function**: кұ°лІ„л„ҢмҠӨ artifact (ОІ-issue body / spec / change-plan / PR body / ADR amendment ліёл¬ё) м•Ҳм—җм„ң нҠ№м • ADR лҳҗлҠ” inter-plugin contract мқҳ amendment лІҲнҳёлҘј мқёмҡ©н•  л•Ң, мқёмҡ© м§Ғм „ target artifact мқҳ frontmatter `amendments:` лӘ©лЎқ (лҳҗлҠ” `amendment_log`) мқ„ `Read` лҸ„кө¬лЎң м§Ғм ‘ нҷ•мқён•ң нӣ„ **м •нҷ• next-slot `M = max(amendment_id) + 1` л§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ**. `M > max + 1` (forward-staleness вҖ” off-by-one / кі„мӮ° мҳӨлҘҳ) лҳҗлҠ” `M вүӨ max` (backward-staleness вҖ” мқҙлҜё land лҗң slot мқёмҡ©) лӘЁл‘җ stale citation (Amendment 7 нҷ•мһҘ, CFP-1312).

**verify-before-cite мқҳл¬ҙ**:

1. target ADR / contract нҢҢмқјмқҳ frontmatter `amendments:` лҳҗлҠ” `amendment_log` н•ӯлӘ©мқ„ м§Ғм ‘ Read н•ңлӢӨ.
2. нҳ„мһ¬ мөңлҢҖ `amendment_id` к°’ (`max`) мқ„ нҷ•мқён•ңлӢӨ.
3. мғҲ amendment лІҲнҳё = **м •нҷ•нһҲ `max + 1`** лЎң кІ°м •н•ңлӢӨ (Amendment 7 лӘ…мӢң вҖ” `M = max+1` мҷё лӘЁл‘җ stale). forward (M > max+1) / backward (M вүӨ max) м–‘л°©н–Ҙ staleness м°ЁлӢЁ.
4. мқёмҡ© мң„м№ҳм—җ `verified-via: <frontmatter Read кІҪлЎң л°Ҹ мӢңк°Ғ>` annotation мқ„ л¶Җм°©н•ңлӢӨ (В§кІ°м • 2(b) `[verified: git show origin/main:<path>]` annotation нҳ•мӢқ мӨҖмҡ©).

**scope**: ліё В§кІ°м • 9 лҠ” В§кІ°м • 2(b) ("ArchitectAgent В§3 / В§7 corpus enumeration + ADR frontmatter value мқёмҡ© мӢң verify") мқҳ sub-specialization мқҙлӢӨ. В§кІ°м • 2(b) к°Җ мқҙлҜё "ADR frontmatter value мқёмҡ© мӢң verify" лҘј нҸ¬кҙ„н•ҳлӮҳ, amendment лІҲнҳё citation мқҙ plan-time (ОІ-issue / spec / change-plan мһ‘м„ұ мӢңм җ) м—җ л°ңмғқн•ҳлҠ” м җ вҖ” мҰү В§кІ°м • 2(b) мқҳ lane agent write-time ліҙлӢӨ мқҙлҘё мӢңм җ вҖ” мқ„ лӘ…мӢңм ҒмңјлЎң м–ёкёүн•ҳкё° мң„н•ҙ лі„лҸ„ кІ°м •мңјлЎң codify.

**м Ғмҡ© лҢҖмғҒ layer**:

| artifact мў…лҘҳ | мЈјмІҙ | м Ғмҡ© layer |
|---|---|---|
| ОІ-issue body, ADR brainstorm Phase 0 spec, change-plan | Orchestrator-authored | ADR-073 (Orchestrator verify-before-assert) вҲ© ліё В§кІ°м • 9 лҸҷмӢң м Ғмҡ© |
| ADR amendment ліёл¬ё, design lane Change Plan | ArchitectAgent (internal lane agent) authored | ліё ADR В§кІ°м • 2(b) + В§кІ°м • 9 лҸҷмӢң м Ғмҡ© |
| spec / plan кё°нғҖ planning artifact | н•ҙлӢ№ lane PL authored | ліё В§кІ°м • 9 м Ғмҡ© |

**disjoint layer кҙҖкі„**: ОІ-issue = Orchestrator-authored artifact мқҙлҜҖлЎң ADR-073 В§кІ°м • 1 (Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify) к°Җ лҸҷмӢң м Ғмҡ©лҗңлӢӨ. лӢЁ, ADR-073 мҷҖ ліё ADR мқҳ axis disjoint (verify subject: Orchestrator cross-repo state assertion вҶ” internal lane agent self-write value assertion) к°Җ ліё В§кІ°м • 9 мқҳ plan-time мҳҒм—ӯм—җм„ң overlap н•ҳлҠ” кө¬мЎ°мһ„мқ„ лӘ…мӢң вҖ” к°Ғ ADR scope м№ЁлІ” м•„лӢҳ (лҸҷмқј artifact м—җ л‘җ layer к°Җ лҸ…лҰҪм ҒмңјлЎң м Ғмҡ©). ADR-073 cross-ref: `docs/adr/ADR-073-orchestrator-verify-before-assert.md` В§кІ°м • 1 (Orchestrator verify-before-assert вҖ” ОІ-issue мһ‘м„ұ мӢң amendment лІҲнҳё cite к°Җ cross-repo state assertion м—җ н•ҙлӢ№).

**known-limitation**: ліё В§кІ°м • 9 = behavioral directive (Wave 1). Wave 2 mechanical lint (`amendment-number-frontmatter-verify` script + workflow + bats fixture) = CFP-1216 Phase 2 (лі„лҸ„ sub-carrier лЎң land мҷ„лЈҢ, 2026-05-22 KST). **Amendment 7 (CFP-1312)** к°Җ Wave 2 lint Check (b) coverage gap (forward only вҶ’ м–‘л°©н–Ҙ) ліҙк°• вҖ” `cited_m != max_id + 1` м–‘л°©н–Ҙ л№„көҗ + `[FORWARD-STALE]` / `[BACKWARD-STALE]` м¶ңл Ҙ format л¶„лҰ¬ + self-reference exemption (ADR file мһҗмІҙ) + templates/** path filter. frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions:` мқҳ `amendment-number-frontmatter-verify` entry status warning retain (scope expand only, tier ліҖкІҪ 0).

**pattern evidence (ADR-045 В§D-9 Mandatory, pattern_count = 3 вҖ” Amendment 7 нҷ•мһҘ)**:

| # | м¶ңмІҳ | stale citation | actual (verified) | staleness л°©н–Ҙ | catch layer |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | CFP-1177 ОІ-issue (#1115) | "ADR-027 Amendment 7" | ADR-027 мӢӨм ң max = Amendment 8 (CFP-1059 м җмң ) вҶ’ мӢӨм ң slot = Amendment 9 | forward (M > max+1) | Amendment 6 Wave 1 behavioral catch |
| 2 | CFP-1179 ОІ-issue (#1114) | "ADR-063 Amendment 6/7" | ADR-063 мӢӨм ң max = Amendment 7 (CFP-906/CFP-1059 м җмң ) вҶ’ мӢӨм ң slot = Amendment 8 | forward (M > max+1) | Amendment 6 Wave 1 behavioral catch |
| 3 | CFP-1293 retro (#1293) | "ADR-083 Amendment 2" | ADR-083 мӢӨм ң max = Amendment 2 мӢңм җ, м •нҷ• next-slot = 3 вҶ’ cited_m=2 вүӨ max=2 | backward (M вүӨ max) | Amendment 6 Wave 1 catch + CFP-1216 lint Check (b) forward-only coverage gap escape вҖ” **Amendment 7 motivation** |

м„ё мјҖмқҙмҠӨ лӘЁл‘җ write-time м—җ caught (plan land нӣ„ escaped 0) мқҙлӮҳ, root cause = (1)/(2) plan-time read verify л¶Җмһ¬ + (3) lint coverage gap (`M > max+1` forward-only л№„көҗ). Amendment 7 = м–‘л°©н–Ҙ mechanical wire ліҙк°• (Wave 2 escape catch).

**ADR-068 I-4 (wording SSOT) м—°кі„**: amendment лІҲнҳёлҠ” governance artifact м „мІҙм—җм„ң лҸҷмқј мӢқлі„мһҗлЎң м°ёмЎ°лҗҳлҠ” wording SSOT лҢҖмғҒмқҙлӢӨ. stale лІҲнҳёк°Җ planning artifact м—җ кё°лЎқлҗҳл©ҙ нӣ„мҶҚ ADR ліёл¬ё / CLAUDE.md / retro мҷҖ wording drift к°Җ л°ңмғқ вҖ” I-4 мң„л°ҳ мӣҗмқёмқҙ лҗңлӢӨ.

### В§кІ°м • 10 вҖ” ArchitectAgent write-time discipline 4 sub-scope expansion (Amendment 8 мӢ м„Ө, CFP-1329)

ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) + В§кІ°м • 2 scope (a-d) (internal lane agent self-write scope) мқҳ write-time verify mandate к°Җ ArchitectAgent (codeforge-design chief author) мқҳ 4 write-time discipline мҳҒм—ӯк№Ңм§Җ нҷ•мһҘ м Ғмҡ©лҗңлӢӨ. 4 sub-decisions лӘЁл‘җ лі„лҸ„ axis disjoint мқҙл©°, к°ҷмқҖ super-class (verify-before-trust write-time semantic truth) м•„лһҳ лӢЁмқј carrier нҶөн•© (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 5 unitary м •н•©).

#### В§кІ°м • 10.A вҖ” Codex TP#2 inline FIX 8-anchor mirror coverage checklist

**carrier**: memory `feedback_codex_tp2_verify_before_trust_pattern` (CFP-795 F-1 lesson)

ArchitectAgent В§3 м§Ғнӣ„ mandatory Codex proactive check touchpoint #2 (ADR-052 Amendment 4) verified-true P1 finding inline FIX мӢң лӢӨмқҢ 8 anchor лҸҷмӢң к°ұмӢ  мқҳл¬ҙ:

1. Change Plan В§3 (mechanical кө¬нҳ„ м„Өкі„ SSOT вҖ” primary anchor)
2. Change Plan В§4 Risk (R-N row append)
3. Change Plan В§7 Threat model (T-N row + В§7.6 л§Өн•‘)
4. Change Plan В§10 (лҜён•ҙмҶҢ deputy мқҙкІ¬ вҖ” finding мқҙн–ү м¶”м Ғ)
5. Story В§7 mirror (Change Plan В§7 mirror мҳҒм—ӯ)
6. ADR amendment_log entry лҒқ (carrier reference 1-line)
7. **ADR ліёл¬ё В§кІ°м • N н‘ңВ·лӢЁлқҪ вҖ” F-1 lesson, лҲ„лқҪ мһҗмЈј л°ңмғқ anchor**
8. ADR мӢ к·ң В§кІ°м • N ліёл¬ё (мЎ°кұҙ / м•Ңкі лҰ¬мҰҳ / fail-closed)

verbatim wording мқјкҙҖ вҖ” ADR-068 I-4 wording SSOT к°•м ң. CFP-795 lesson: 8-mirror coverage к°Җ default мҳҖлӢӨл©ҙ iter 1 нҡҢн”ј.

**sentinel codify rationale** (pattern_count 1): CFP-795 F-1 dogfood inversion P1 prevention. forward-prevention лҸ„кө¬м Ғ к°Җм№ҳ > recurrence вүҘ 2 wait вҖ” ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 м •н•© (sentinel forward-prevention мҳҒм—ӯ м ҒкІ©, ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 7 CFP-1149 Amendment 8 symmetric evidence-gated л©ҙм ң вҖ” лҸ„кө¬м Ғ к°Җм№ҳ evidence base).

#### В§кІ°м • 10.B вҖ” Mid-author partial revert propagation gap

**carrier**: memory `feedback_mid_author_partial_revert_propagation_gap` (CFP-1009 F-DR-001 P1 dogfood inversion sentinel)

mid-author Codex TP catch + inline FIX body normative correction м§Ғнӣ„ frontmatter inline comment / appendix narrative / table cell sync мҳҒм—ӯк№Ңм§Җ propagation мқҳл¬ҙ:

1. ArchitectPL mid-author FIX м§Ғнӣ„ self-discipline: `grep -rn "<stale-label>" <touched-files>` cross-check (wider scope frontmatter comment + appendix + table cell)
2. DesignReviewPL mandatory audit point вҖ” body normative correction вҶ” frontmatter inline comment + appendix + table cell мқјкҙҖм„ұ verify
3. post-FIX reverse-mutual grep cross-check мқҳл¬ҙ (to-remove pattern grep = 0 in target + to-add pattern grep вүҘ N)

**sentinel codify rationale**: pattern_count 1 (CFP-1009 dogfood inversion P1). evidence-gate wait лҢҖмӢ  forward prevention к°Җм№ҳ мҡ°м„  вҖ” ADR-074 carrier ADR мһҗмІҙ к°ҷмқҖ defect ліҙмң  = dogfood inversion P1 severity, recurrence вүҘ 2 wait мӢң P1 мһ¬л°ң risk. ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 forward-prevention мҳҒм—ӯ м ҒкІ© (лҸ„кө¬м Ғ к°Җм№ҳ > wait, ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 7 CFP-1149 Amendment 8 symmetric evidence-gated л©ҙм ң).

#### В§кІ°м • 10.C вҖ” ArchitectAgent self-introduced script-behavior claim verify

**carrier**: memory `feedback_architect_script_behavior_claim_verify` (pattern_count 2 reach)

ArchitectAgent (or Combined Req+Design lane) authors a claim about codeforge-internal script behavior (e.g., "parse-X.py skips template entries", "bootstrap-labels.sh creates all labels") = write-time self-introduced assertion. мқҳл¬ҙ empirical verify:

1. ArchitectAgent self-discipline (best-effort): codeforge script behavior claim мһ‘м„ұ мӢң `[verified-via: <command>]` annotation + empirical command run + result лӘ…мӢң. лҜёverify мӢң `[unverified вҖ” DesignReview to confirm]` лӘ…мӢң.
2. DesignReviewPL mandatory audit point: Story / Change Plan / ADR text м•Ҳ script behavior assertion мӢң dedicated audit point м¶”к°Җ вҖ” script мӢӨн–ү + source grep verify.
3. mutual cross-check before declaring iter complete (F-DR-1006-3 lesson): systematic wording correction м Ғмҡ© мӢң to-remove pattern + to-add pattern м–‘ axis grep cross-check мқҳл¬ҙ.

**pattern_count 2 evidence**:

| # | Story | claim | actual (verified) | severity |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | CFP-1006 F-DR-1006-1 (P2) | parse-hotfix-bypass-labels.py "skips template entry" | actual gh-side rejection (mechanism mismatch) | P2 dogfood gap |
| 2 | CFP-1025 (Orchestrator hypothesis REFUTED by ArchitectPL empirical verify) | hypothesis л°ңнҷ” | pattern WORKING dogfood win | P3 hypothesis refuted |

**scope**: В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) + ліё В§кІ°м • 10.C (ArchitectAgent scope) м–‘ layer лҸҷмӢң м Ғмҡ© вҖ” RequirementsPL В§2.1 verified state table мқҙ cover м•Ҳ н•ҳлҠ” "script behavior assertion at write-time" disjoint gap. ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope (1-A Amendment 1 base / 1-B Amendment 2 CFP-1016 Issue-body authorship / 1-C Amendment 5 CFP-1110 lane PL spawn prompt user-utterance verbatim) вҶ’ ліё В§кІ°м • 10.C = ArchitectAgent chief author scope м¶”к°Җ layer. **FIX iter 1 м •м • (DesignReview F-2 P0)**: stale "Amendment 3" citation м •м • вҖ” verify-before-cite mandate (Amendment 7 В§кІ°м • 9) self-application мӮ¬лЎҖ.

#### В§кІ°м • 10.D вҖ” META self-application pattern

**carrier**: memory `feedback_meta_self_application_pattern` (pattern_count 2 reach)

Story introduces template / codification change вҶ’ apply it to carrier Story itself as 1st applied case (eat your own dog food):

1. ArchitectPL Amendment / template / mandate change мӢң мһҗл¬ё: "Does this codification apply to a Story that I am writing right now?"
2. yes мӢң: Story file мһҗмІҙм—җ м Ғмҡ© (frontmatter field + мӢ к·ң section + мӢ к·ң procedure verbatim)
3. META self-application лӘ…мӢң:
   - ADR amendment body: `## Amendment N` м•Ҳ "Meta-self-application" sub-section
   - Change Plan В§11 кІ°лЎ : "carrier Story applies the codification as 1st case"
   - Story В§2.1 / В§3 / В§9: META context cross-ref
4. DesignReviewPL audit: META self-application validation dedicated audit point

### В§кІ°м • 11 вҖ” Code-level write-time semantic truth verify expansion (Amendment 9 мӢ м„Ө, CFP-1330)

ADR-082 super-class (write-time semantic truth verify) scope к°Җ Code-level write-time discipline 2 sub-scope (test code production binding + script error visibility) мҳҒм—ӯк№Ңм§Җ нҷ•мһҘ м Ғмҡ©лҗңлӢӨ. Amendment 8 В§кІ°м • 10 (ArchitectAgent write-time discipline) кіј disjoint axis вҖ” Amendment 8 = кұ°лІ„л„ҢмҠӨ artifact write-time / ліё В§кІ°м • 11 = мҪ”л“ң artifact (test/script) write-time. к°ҷмқҖ super-class (write-time semantic truth) м•„лһҳ лӢЁмқј carrier нҶөн•© (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 5 unitary м •н•©).

#### В§кІ°м • 11.A вҖ” Test code production binding verify

**carrier**: memory `feedback_test_must_bind_to_production` (CFP-1025 F-CR-1025-2 sentinel)

bug-fix bats/unit test = real production code source/exec мқҳл¬ҙ (sed-extract real fn, NOT inline hand-copy). Inline-copy = tautology, zero regression binding (test к°Җ мһҗкё° мһҗмӢ мқ„ кІҖмҰқн•ҳлҠ” нҳ•нғңлЎң production code ліҖкІҪ мӢң silent regression coverage gap).

**мқҳл¬ҙ м Ҳм°Ё**:

1. **DeveloperPL / QADev**: regression test к°Җ real artifact source/exec:
   - bash function: `sed -n '/^funcname() {/,/^}/p' "${SCRIPT}" > _fn.sh; source _fn.sh` (sed-extract real fn)
   - whole script: DRY_RUN / early-return hook мңјлЎң target function л§Ң stub лҢҖмғҒ мӢӨн–ү
   - **NEVER re-type / inline fixed logic** (hand-copy = tautology smell)
2. **Discriminating-fixture (RED proof)**: sed-substitute bug INTO extracted real function (e.g., `2>&1` вҶ’ `2>/dev/null`), source THAT, assert test FAILS. hand-written buggy variant = tautology.
3. **CodeReviewPL audit point**: `[ -f $SCRIPT ]` existence-only guard + inline function body + hand-written `*_masked` / `*_mock` reimplementation tautology smell grep. P1 severity (test-quality regression).
4. **Acceptance**: production fix manual revert вҶ’ test RED. мһ”мЎҙ GREEN вҶ’ tautology, unresolved.

**sentinel codify rationale** (pattern_count 1): CFP-1025 F-CR-1025-2 dogfood inversion. forward-prevention к°Җм№ҳ мҡ°м„  (test-quality defect = silent regression coverage gap, recurrence вүҘ 2 wait мӢң silent regression risk). ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 forward-prevention мҳҒм—ӯ м ҒкІ© (лҸ„кө¬м Ғ к°Җм№ҳ evidence base, ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 7 CFP-1149 Amendment 8 symmetric evidence-gated л©ҙм ң).

#### В§кІ°м • 11.B вҖ” Script error visibility audit

**carrier**: memory `feedback_error_mask_metaroot` (CFP-1025 bootstrap-labels.sh:53-55 META-ROOT sentinel)

Script `2>/dev/null` к°Җ success/failure ліҙкі н•ҳл©ҙм„ң real error л§ҲмҠӨнӮ№ = **mis-diagnosis amplifier META-ROOT**. False-success к°Җ downstream Story mis-diagnose мң л°ң + Wave-defer rationale falsify (CFP-1006 mis-diagnosis lineage downstream propagation verified).

**мқҳл¬ҙ м Ҳм°Ё**:

1. **Design lane / ArchitectAgent**: лҰ¬мҶҢмҠӨ create / state change ліҙкі  script мһ‘м„ұ мӢң `2>/dev/null` кёҲм§Җ (error path). `err=$(cmd 2>&1)` нҳ•нғңлЎң stderr capture + failure мӢң verbatim surface. `2>/dev/null` мҳҒм—ӯ = м§„м • benign expected-noise (мҳҲ: `command -v` probes) only вҖ” success/failure consumed downstream operations мҳҒм—ӯ кёҲм§Җ.
2. **Root-cause м§„лӢЁ discipline**: predecessor Story assumption falsified мӢң masked-error META-ROOT мқҳмӢ¬. RAW signal (workflow run log, NOT script summary; admin probe, NOT CI token masked result) prior hypothesis нҳ•м„ұ м „.
3. **CodeReview / SecurityTest audit**: `Grep '2>/dev/null' scripts/**` resource-creating/state-changing commands. mis-diagnosis-amplifier risk н‘ңмӢң (severity scales by downstream consumer мҲҳ).

**META-ROOT pattern_count 1** (CFP-1025 bootstrap-labels.sh:53-55): codify rationale forward-prevention (META-ROOT severity = mis-diagnosis м „нҢҢ chain risk, recurrence вүҘ 2 wait мӢң P1 propagation мҳҒм—ӯ вҖ” CFP-1006 mis-diagnosis lineage verified). codeforge-wide grep audit = follow-up CFP carrier (лі„лҸ„ sweep). ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 forward-prevention мҳҒм—ӯ м ҒкІ©, ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 7 CFP-1149 Amendment 8 symmetric evidence-gated л©ҙм ң.

#### В§кІ°м • 11 вҖ” disjoint axis with Amendment 8 В§кІ°м • 10

| Amendment | scope | write-time artifact axis | layer |
|---|---|---|---|
| Amendment 8 В§кІ°м • 10 | ArchitectAgent write-time discipline 4 sub-scope (A/B/C/D) | кұ°лІ„л„ҢмҠӨ artifact (Story / Change Plan / ADR / memory) | governance write-time |
| **Amendment 9 В§кІ°м • 11** | **Code-level write-time discipline 2 sub-scope (A/B)** | **мҪ”л“ң artifact (test code / script error path)** | **code write-time** |

л‘җ Amendment к°Җ ADR-082 super-class (write-time semantic truth verify) мқҳ disjoint layer expansion. Amendment 8 = chief author scope / Amendment 9 = Code-level scope. CFP scope unitary (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 5) м •н•© вҖ” лӢЁмқј super-class м•Ҳ disjoint axis л¶„лҰ¬.

**Wave 1 = declaration-only**: 2 sub-decisions лӘЁл‘җ behavioral directive. Wave 2 mechanical wire (CodeReviewPL audit dedicated points: tautology smell grep + `Grep '2>/dev/null' scripts/**` resource-creating/state-changing audit + codeforge-wide grep audit sweep) = лі„лҸ„ sub-carrier л¶„лҰ¬ (deferred-followup, ADR-082 Wave 1 declaration-only precedent лӢөмҠө).

**META-self-application (В§кІ°м • 10.D 4th applied case)**: ліё Amendment 9 мһҗмІҙк°Җ В§кІ°м • 10.D pattern self-applied вҖ” ліё Amendment лІҲнҳё 9 к°Җ target ADR-082 frontmatter `amendments:` лӘ©лЎқ Read verify нӣ„ max(8)+1=9 мңјлЎң кІ°м • (verified-via: Read worktree `docs/adr/ADR-082-...md` frontmatter `amendments[]` L11-51 max=8, 2026-05-24 KST кё°мӨҖ origin/main a0eb545 вҖ” CFP-1329 Amendment 8 merge нӣ„ base). ### В§кІ°м • 12 вҖ” RequirementsPL + retro-time verify-before-trust 2 sub-scope expansion (Amendment 10 мӢ м„Ө, CFP-1332)

ADR-082 super-class write-time semantic truth verify scope к°Җ (a) RequirementsPL В§2.1 verified state table mandate strengthening + (b) retro-time empirical verify (Wave-defer rationale falsification м°ЁлӢЁ) м–‘ axis лҸҷмӢң expansion. write-time-only вҶ’ write-time + retro-time lifecycle.

#### В§кІ°м • 12.A вҖ” Orchestrator-authored Issue body В§2.1 verified state table mandate strengthening

**carrier**: memory `feedback_issue_body_verify_before_trust` (pattern_count 2 reach вҖ” CFP-1000 INVERSE drift + CFP-1001 lint output FP)

Orchestrator к°Җ follow-up CFP batch Issue body author мӢң (e.g., post-retro batch creation) Issue body claim мқҙ parallel-session merge мӮ¬мқҙ stale / factually inverted к°ҖлҠҘ. RequirementsPL spawn prompt **MUST include explicit verify-before-trust mandate** on each Issue body claim:

1. Reproduce any cited lint output via direct script invocation in worktree
2. Direct file Read for cited line numbers (line numbers may have shifted post-parallel-merge)
3. Direct gh CLI/API probe for cited gh-side state (label existence, baseline count, registry value)
4. Direct file existence check for cited paths (e.g., `.claude-work/` directory)

**В§2.1 verified state table mandatory** (ADR-082 Amendment 2 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 strengthening, frontmatter `issue_origin: orchestrator_authored_followup` мқҳл¬ҙ codify). Both layers preserved: В§1 verbatim Issue (immutable, story-section-1-immutable.yml) + В§2 verified state (drives downstream lanes).

**pattern_count 2 evidence**:
- CFP-1000 вҖ” Issue body claim "prod-cutover-deputy-evidence not registered in gh" verified state INVERSE = REGISTERED in gh, MISSING in registry (Pivot detected, fix direction м •м •)
- CFP-1001 вҖ” Issue body cite "L189 ADR-038 Amendment 6 lint output as drift" verified state = lint regex cross-context window Вұ5-line false-pair (paired with L185 ADR-040 Amendment 6, NOT a real drift)

#### В§кІ°м • 12.B вҖ” Retro-time wave_defer empirical verify

**carrier**: memory `feedback_wave_defer_empirical_verify` (pattern_count 2 reach вҖ” CFP-1006 Wave-defer rationale falsified + CFP-1025 corrective closure pattern WORKING)

Story к°Җ sub-scope Wave 2/3 follow-up CFP лЎң defer мӢң rationale "will auto-resolve via mechanism X" = **retro time м—җ empirical verify мқҳл¬ҙ** (Story-write time к°Җм • кёҲм§Җ). Wave-defer = ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1 scope-unitary м •н•© practice, лӢЁ deferral *reason* мқҙ hypothesis ("mechanism X handles it automatically") мқё кІҪмҡ° FALSE к°ҖлҠҘм„ұ кІҖмҰқ мқҳл¬ҙ.

**мқҳл¬ҙ м Ҳм°Ё** (retro time PMOAgent / Orchestrator):
1. Wave-deferred sub-scope л§ҲлӢӨ deferral rationale мқҙ predict н•ҳлҠ” empirical check мӢӨн–ү:
   - "auto-resolves via workflow X" вҶ’ workflow X к°Җ post-merge actual produced state predicted state мқјм№ҳ verify
   - "covered by existing lint Y" вҶ’ lint Y мӢӨн–ү, deferred concern catch нҷ•мқё
   - "backward-compat preserved" вҶ’ backward-compat scenario actual run
2. Retro м•Ҳ empirical result кё°лЎқ:
   - нҷ•мқё вҶ’ Wave N follow-up к°Җ precautionary/optional (deprioritize к°ҖлҠҘ)
   - л°ҳмҰқ вҶ’ Wave N follow-up к°Җ genuinely required (priority кІ©мғҒ + м •нҷ• root cause re-diagnose)

**pattern_count 2 evidence**:
- CFP-1006 Wave 1 вҖ” "36 registryвҶ’gh missing entries auto-resolve via bootstrap-labels.yml CFP-598 dynamic registry-driven pattern on PR open" rationale post-merge verify: gh hotfix-bypass label count 15 unchanged from pre-CFP-1006 вҶ’ rationale FALSIFIED. Wave 2 = Issue #1025 genuinely required (not precautionary)
- CFP-1025 вҖ” empirical diagnosis via raw `gh run view 26080174058 --log` REFUTED Orchestrator's pre-spawn PyYAML hypothesis (115 blanket failures = 2-layer token-gap + error-mask META-ROOT). empirical-verify discipline prevented second mis-diagnosis (pattern WORKING AS DESIGNED)

### В§кІ°м • 13 вҖ” GitOps verify-before-trust discipline 3 sub-scope expansion (Amendment 11 мӢ м„Ө, CFP-1338)

ADR-082 super-class verify-before-trust scope к°Җ GitOps coordination layer мҳҒм—ӯ expansion вҖ” main drift bypass audit + HEAD SHA pin + branch protection worktree cleanup 3 sub-scope.

#### В§кІ°м • 13.A вҖ” Main drift bypass audit pattern (pattern_count 5 reach HIGH)

**carrier**: memory `feedback_main_drift_bypass_audit_pattern` вҖ” codeforge wrapper PR к°Җ pre-existing main drift лҘј inherit мӢң н‘ңмӨҖ 4 hotfix-bypass labels + [bypass-justification] audit comment template м Ғмҡ© (per ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1 scope unitary м •н•©).

**мқҳл¬ҙ м Ҳм°Ё**:
1. Pre-merge verify-before-trust: к°Ғ failing non-required check лҘј CFP-N-introduced vs pre-existing main drift л¶„лҘҳ вҖ” direct git diff inspection
2. 4 н‘ңмӨҖ hotfix-bypass labels gh CLI м Ғмҡ© (failure мҳҒм—ӯ лі„):
   - `hotfix-bypass:marketplace-description-verbatim` (CFP-1286~ description sync gap)
   - `hotfix-bypass:wording-dictionary` (CHANGELOG.md pre-existing 'ratchet' / 'pin' / 'лі„' standalone advisory)
   - `hotfix-bypass:inter-plugin-contracts-parity` (CFP-1059 deploy_output / deploy_review_output canonical л¶Җмһ¬)
   - `hotfix-bypass:marketplace-atomic` (description-verbatim sister)
3. `[bypass-justification]` marker comment (comment-prefix-registry-v1 v1.3 14th prefix, CFP-845 carrier): per-finding root cause + verify-before-trust evidence + ADR-024 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 6.C audit trail mandate cross-ref
4. pattern_count tracking in PMO retro section (вүҘ 2 same drift class = ADR escalation candidate)

**pattern_count 5 reach evidence**: CFP-963 P1+P2 + CFP-1000 + CFP-1001 + CFP-1340/1329/1330/1332 batch (4 bypass label лҸҷмӢң м Ғмҡ© lineage). HIGH evidence вҖ” sentinel мҳҒм—ӯ м•„лӢҳ (standard pattern_count reach).

#### В§кІ°м • 13.B вҖ” HEAD SHA pin step 0 (verify-before-trust precondition)

**carrier**: memory `feedback_verify_pin_head_sha` (CFP-722 stale HEAD verification churn sentinel)

Async multi-agent coordination м•Ҳ branch artifact verify-before-trust мӢң мқҳл¬ҙ:

1. **Step 0**: `gh api repos/<owner>/<repo>/commits/<branch> --jq '.sha'` мңјлЎң current HEAD н•ҙкІ°, к·ё SHA pin
2. **Content verify**: `?ref=<pinned-sha>` нҳ•мӢқмңјлЎң pinned SHA м•Ҳ content verify (mid-chain SHA / agent self-claim SHA blind verify кёҲм§Җ вҖ” branch к°Җ advanced к°ҖлҠҘ)
3. **Incremental commit signal мӢң**: explicit HEAD re-resolve (incremental commit = stale-HEAD trigger)
4. **Stale REJECT correction**: stale SHA against correct REJECT лҸ„ process error вҶ’ мӢ мҶҚ withdraw (spurious re-FIX churn нҡҢн”ј)

**sentinel codify rationale**: CFP-722 evidence single occurrence. ADR-073 verify-before-assert sub-discipline cross-ref-sufficient. Codify rationale = forward-prevention (verifier мқҳ stale-ref churn risk м°ЁлӢЁ).

#### В§кІ°м • 13.C вҖ” Branch protection нҷҳкІҪ worktree cleanup мҲңм„ң

**carrier**: memory `feedback_branch_protection_worktree_cleanup` (workflow discipline)

Main branch protection active repo мҳҒм—ӯ finishing-a-development-branch skill мӢӨн–ү мӢң:

1. Option 1 (Merge Locally) м ңмӢң кёҲм§Җ (main protect мӢң `git merge` + `git push` м§Ғм ‘ л°ҳмҳҒ л¶Ҳк°Җ)
2. Option 2 (Push + PR) м„ нғқ нӣ„ worktree = **PR merge нҷ•мқё нӣ„** лі„лҸ„ м •лҰ¬
3. PR merge нҷ•мқё = `gh pr view <number> --json mergedAt` лҳҗлҠ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ нҷ•мқё
4. codeforge plugin-codeforge repo н•ӯмғҒ м Ғмҡ© (ADR-024 branch protection к°•м ң) + consumer repo к¶ҢмһҘ (consumer-guide В§2e)

**workflow discipline codify rationale**: branch protection нҷҳкІҪ timing convention м •мқҳ вҖ” premature worktree removal мӢң PR н”јл“ңл°ұ лҢҖмқ‘ л¶Ҳк°Җ + late removal мӢң м¶”м Ғ л¶Ҳк°Җ. ADR-024 + ADR-040 cross-ref.

| Amendment | scope | verify lifecycle axis | layer |
|---|---|---|---|
| Amendment 8 В§кІ°м • 10 | ArchitectAgent write-time discipline 4 sub-scope | governance artifact write-time | governance write-time |
| Amendment 9 В§кІ°м • 11 | Code-level write-time discipline 2 sub-scope | code artifact write-time | code write-time |
| Amendment 10 В§кІ°м • 12 | RequirementsPL + retro-time verify expansion | Issue-body + retro-time | lifecycle expansion |
| **Amendment 11 В§кІ°м • 13** | **GitOps verify-before-trust discipline 3 sub-scope** | **bypass audit + HEAD SHA pin + worktree cleanup** | **GitOps coordination** |

4 Amendment лӘЁл‘җ ADR-082 super-class (verify-before-trust mandate) мқҳ disjoint axis expansion. CFP scope unitary (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 5) м •н•©.

**META-self-application (В§кІ°м • 10.D 6th applied case)**: ліё Amendment 11 мһҗмІҙк°Җ В§кІ°м • 10.D pattern self-applied вҖ” ліё Amendment лІҲнҳё 11 = max(10)+1 (verified-via Read frontmatter L11-65 max=10 origin/main e7b7791).

## кІ°кіј

ліё ADR codify кІ°кіј:

- ADR-073 (Orchestrator cross-repo) + ADR-070 (Codex external worker) disjoint super-class layer мӢ м„Ө вҖ” internal lane agent self-write write-time semantic truth verify
- В§кІ°м • 1 layer disjoint 4-layer н‘ң = 4 ADR кіөнҶө anchor (over-abstraction мҡ°л Ө мҷ„нҷ” вҖ” domain-knowledge кіөл°ұ = мӢ к·ң layer м •лӢ№)
- В§кІ°м • 2 scope (a-d) write-time verify мқҳл¬ҙ + 4 corpus pattern м§Ғм ‘ л§Өн•‘ м°ЁлӢЁ
- В§кІ°м • 3 м •м • мһ¬к·Җ verify + ADR-067 кІ°м • 1 (max FIX 3/3 reassessment trigger) + кІ°м • 3 (RESET vs escalation к¶Ңн•ң) ліөн•© мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© (л¬ҙн•ңлЈЁн”„ м°ЁлӢЁ мӢ к·ң л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ лҜёлҸ„мһ…)
- В§кІ°м • 4 citation вү  assertion кІҪкі„ (over-verify нҡҢн”ј вҖ” мқёмҡ©мқҖ verify л©ҙм ң)
- В§кІ°м • 5 provisional marker defer (planning-phase л°ҳліө cost нҡҢн”ј)
- В§кІ°м • 6 `mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` known-limitation rationale binding (ADR-040 Amendment 3 missing flag нҡҢн”ј) + нӣ„мҶҚ carrier л°ңмқҳ мқҳл¬ҙ + self-referential trap нҡҢн”ј self-protection (EC-3)
- ADR-073/070 Amendment 1 cross-ref (disjoint ліҙмҷ„ 1мӨ„) + ADR-045 Amendment 6 (В§D-9 м Ғмҡ© evidence 1мӨ„)
- ADR-RESERVATION row 82 active (CFP-776, reserved лҜёкІҪмң  м§Ғм ‘ active = ADR-079/080/081 row precedent м •н•©)
- CLAUDE.md verify-before-trust лӢЁлқҪ ADR-082 мӢ мһ… + 4-layer кі„мёө + playbook В§3.10/В§3.14 cross-ref 1мӨ„ append-safe
- ліё carrier мһҗмІҙ = PMOAgent ADR-045 В§D-9 pattern_count 3 вүҘ threshold 2 forcing function мӮ°л¬ј (escalation_action escalate_user вҶ’ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӢЁмқј super-class нҶөн•© кІ°м •)

## кұ°м Ҳлҗң лҢҖм•Ҳ

- **(D-A) scope (e) ліё ADR нқЎмҲҳ** вҖ” disjoint кҙҖмӢ¬мӮ¬ (fix-event-v1 schema ліҖкІҪ лҸҷл°ҳ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ), CFP-scope-unitary мң„л°ҳ вҶ’ В§кІ°м • 7 лі„лҸ„ CFP л¶„лҰ¬.
- **(D-B) per-area л¶„н•  (scope a/b/c/d к°Ғ лі„лҸ„ ADR)** вҖ” super-class anchor 4 ADR л¶„м Ҳ, ADR-045 В§D-9 pattern aggregation м•Ҫнҷ” вҶ’ В§кІ°м • 8 лӢЁмқј super-class кұ°л¶Җ.
- **(D-C) mechanical lint мҰүмӢң enforce (Wave 1 лҸҷмӢң mechanical_enforcement_actions[] мӢ м„Ө)** вҖ” scope (d) verify source mechanical-queryable registry л¶Җмһ¬ (Researcher Unknown #2). Wave 1 mechanical нҷ” мӢң (a) л§Ң л¶Җл¶„ codify вҶ’ super-class anchor л¶„м Ҳ (ADR-040 Amendment 3 self-application Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 progression chain мҶҗмӢӨ). вҶ’ В§кІ°м • 6 behavioral mandate Wave 1 + нӣ„мҶҚ carrier л¶„лҰ¬.
- **(D-D) мӢ к·ң л¬ҙн•ңлЈЁн”„ м°ЁлӢЁ л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ лҸ„мһ… (м •м • мһ¬к·Җ cap мһҗмІҙ мӢ м„Ө)** вҖ” ADR-067 кІ°м • 1 (max FIX 3/3 reassessment trigger) + кІ°м • 3 (RESET vs escalation к¶Ңн•ң) мқҙ лҸ„л©”мқёмғҒ мқҙлҜё мЎҙмһ¬ вҶ’ В§кІ°м • 3 кё°мЎҙ layer мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© (over-engineering нҡҢн”ј).

## Amendment 1 вҖ” В§кІ°м • 6 behavioralвҶ’mechanical м „нҷҳ (CFP-841, 2026-05-17 KST)

### м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

Wave 1 (CFP-776) В§кІ°м • 6 мқҖ `mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` empty лҘј лӘ…мӢңм Ғ known-limitation мңјлЎң кІ°м •н•ҳл©ҙм„ң **нӣ„мҶҚ carrier л°ңмқҳ мқҳл¬ҙ**лҘј ліёл¬ём—җ лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”н–ҲлӢӨ (scope (d) mechanical-queryable registry нҷ” + scope (a) corpus annotation lint = лі„лҸ„/лҸҷмқј нӣ„мҶҚ carrier, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •). CFP-776 retro В§6 нӣ„ліҙ 1 escalation_action `escalate_user` вҶ’ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ "Carrier 6+7 escalation м „мІҙ л°ңмқҳ" мҠ№мқё (2026-05-16 KST). brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м • = scope (a) + scope (d) **лӢЁмқј нҶөн•© carrier** (ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 1 unitary scope вҖ” scope (a) л§Ң л¶Җл¶„ codify мӢң В§кІ°м • 6 rationale 2 super-class anchor л¶„м Ҳ мң„л°ҳ).

### Amendment

#### A1-1 вҖ” `mechanical_enforcement_actions: []` вҶ’ 2-entry deferred-followup

frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions:` empty вҶ’ 2 entry:

| action | target_section | status | Phase 2 carrier |
|---|---|---|---|
| `corpus-claim-verify` | В§кІ°м • 2(a) | deferred-followup | CFP-841 Change Plan В§3.1 вҖ” Story/Change-Plan/ADR corpus enumeration `[verified: git show <ref>:<path>]` annotation lint (ADR-068 I-5 directly-analogous pattern мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©) |
| `cross-plugin-ownership-verify` | В§кІ°м • 2(d) | deferred-followup | CFP-841 Change Plan В§3.2 вҖ” `lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.yaml` cross_plugin_doc_ownership sub-tree query 1-step lint + В§13.B 4-way drift-sync invariant |

status `deferred-followup` = Phase 1 declare / Phase 2 actual wire (ADR-060 В§кІ°м • 5 лӘЁл“  мӢ к·ң entry warning мӢңмһ‘ к°•м ң + ADR-040 Amendment 3 self-application Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 progression chain м •н•©).

#### A1-2 вҖ” В§кІ°м • 6 rationale 1 partial-stale м •м •

Wave 1 rationale 1 "scope 2(d) verify source mechanical-queryable registry нҳ•нғң л¶Җмһ¬" м „м ңлҠ” **partially stale**: `docs/domain-knowledge/domain/governance-principle/lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.yaml` machine_readable_ssot к°Җ CFP-722 В§13.A лЎң мқҙлҜё мӢӨмһ¬ (verified-via: `git show origin/main:skills/lane-self-write-boundary/SKILL.md` L36 + `git show origin/main:docs/domain-knowledge/domain/governance-principle/lane-self-write-ownership-matrix.yaml` sections 1-12). лӢЁ yaml = Story file per-section ownership н•ңм • (ADR/Change Plan/Retro/domain-knowledge cross-plugin doc owner sub-tree л¶Җмһ¬). вҶ’ scope 2(d) = **мӢ к·ң registry м°Ҫм„Ө м•„лӢҢ кё°мЎҙ yaml cross-plugin doc-ownership мҳҒм—ӯ нҷ•мһҘ** (disjoint sub-tree append-only) + lint binding + SKILL.md В§13.B 4-way drift-sync н•ҙмҶҢ. В§кІ°м • 6 rationale 1 ліёл¬ём—җ strikethrough + Amendment 1 м •м • лӘ…л¬ёнҷ” мҷ„лЈҢ.

#### A1-3 вҖ” scope 2(b)/2(c)/2(e) мҳҒм—ӯ мң м§Җ (scope_boundary)

ліё Amendment 1 **нҸ¬н•Ё**: scope 2(a) + scope 2(d) mechanical м „нҷҳ (deferred-followup declare + Phase 2 actual wire carrier).

ліё Amendment 1 **out-of-scope** (мң м§Җ):

- scope 2(b)/2(c) = В§кІ°м • 2 behavioral mandate мҳҒм—ӯ мң м§Җ (super-class anchor мқҳ behavioral forcing function ліҙмЎҙ вҖ” mechanical м „нҷҳ л№„лҢҖмғҒ)
- scope 2(e) = В§кІ°м • 7 лі„лҸ„ CFP л¶„лҰ¬ кІ°м • мң м§Җ (fix-event-v1 schema лҸҷл°ҳ к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ)
- мӢ к·ң ADR м°Ҫм„Ө = Amendment only (ADR-RESERVATION мӢ к·ң row 0)
- I-5 ліёл¬ё м •мұ… ліҖкІҪ = ADR-068 cross-ref only (directly-analogous pattern мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© лӘ…мӢң, Amendment м•„лӢҳ)

### Compatibility

- В§кІ°м • 1~5 + В§кІ°м • 7~8 + В§ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё + В§м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (corpus 4кұҙ) м „л¶Җ мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 1 мқҖ В§кІ°м • 6 мқҳ behavioralвҶ’mechanical м „нҷҳ + rationale 1 м •м • only.

## Amendment 2 вҖ” Orchestrator-authored Issue body pre-publish verify mandate (CFP-1016, 2026-05-19 KST)

### м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

Amendment 1 (CFP-841) нӣ„мҶҚ, В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) мқҳ verify-before-trust м Ғмҡ© лІ”мң„м—җ мғҲлЎңмҡҙ corpus pattern лҲ„м Ғ вҖ” **Orchestrator к°Җ follow-up Issue body лҘј author н•  л•Ң (retro time / brainstorm Phase 0 нӣ„мҶҚ / ADR amendment carrier reservation л“ұ) Issue body ліёл¬ё claim мқ„ source verify м—Ҷмқҙ лӢЁм–ён•ҳлҠ” нҢЁн„ҙмқҙ 3 Story лҲ„м Ғ**. кё°мЎҙ ADR-073 (Orchestrator cross-repo state verify) + ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) лҠ” **lane м§„мһ… мӢң Orchestrator к°Җ мҷёл¶Җ state/assumption мқ„ лӢЁм •н•  л•Ң** verify мқҳл¬ҙлЎң codify. Story В§2.1 row 2 к°Җ sed + ls direct verify лЎң catch (verified-via: `git show origin/main:codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/stories/CFP-1002.md` L38-L67 2026-05-19 KST). |

PMOAgent ADR-045 В§D-9 м •лҹү мһ„кі„к°’: pattern_count **3** вүҘ threshold 2 вҶ’ Mandatory framing + escalation_action `escalate_user`.

**Meta-self-application**: ліё ADR carrier Story (CFP-1016) мқҳ Issue body мһҗмІҙк°Җ Orchestrator-authored at CFP-1002 retro time (2026-05-19 KST). ліё Amendment 2 carrier Story В§2.1 verified state table мқҙ 4 claims (CFP-1000 inversions / CFP-1001 lint output / CFP-1002 filename / ADR-082 next amendment_id) кІҖмҰқ вҖ” eating the dog food. нҢЁн„ҙ 4-occurrence-recovered (4-occurrence-prevent).

### Amendment

#### A2-1 вҖ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) verify scope нҷ•мһҘ (Issue body authorship time)

В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (ADR-073) Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify мқҳ м Ғмҡ© лІ”мң„м—җ **Issue body authorship time** лӘ…мӢңм Ғ codify:

| sub-scope | trigger | verify мқҳл¬ҙ |
|---|---|---|
| (1-A) lane spawn / cross-repo state assertion | lane м§„мһ… мӢң мҷёл¶Җ state лӢЁм • | `git fetch origin` + `git show origin/main:<path>` + `verified-via` annotation (Wave 1 = ADR-073) |
| **(1-B) Orchestrator-authored Issue body claim** | **Orchestrator к°Җ retro time / brainstorm Phase 0 нӣ„мҶҚ / ADR amendment carrier reservation / pattern_count escalation forcing function мӮ°л¬јлЎң Issue body лҘј author н•  л•Ң** | **Issue body м•Ҳ лӘЁл“  `claim` (file path / registry value / lint output / cross-repo state / ADR frontmatter value / amendment count л“ұ) мқ„ source direct verify нӣ„ author. Orchestrator к°Җ Issue body м•Ҳ fact citation мқҳ ground truth лҘј verify-before-trust мқҳл¬ҙ вҖ” Amendment 2 мӢ м„Ө** |

verify mechanism (Wave 1 = behavioral mandate + Wave 1.5 = mechanical-enforceable in Story-level):

1. **behavioral mandate (playbook В§3.17, Wave 1)** вҖ” Orchestrator к°Җ Issue body author мӢң fact claim л§ҲлӢӨ `git show <ref>:<path>` / `grep -c` / `gh issue view` / `mcp__github__get_file_contents` л“ұ direct verify нӣ„ author. body м•Ҳ fact citation м–ҙнңҳ мӮ¬мҡ© мӢң implicit verify мқҳл¬ҙ inherited from В§кІ°м • 2(c) (В§9 evidence write-time verify) directly-analogous pattern.
2. **mechanical-enforceable (templates/story-page-structure.md В§2.1, Wave 1 alternative (a))** вҖ” Story file frontmatter м—җ мӢ к·ң field `issue_origin: orchestrator_authored_followup` (vs default `user_authored_issue_form`) лҸ„мһ…. `issue_origin: orchestrator_authored_followup` мӢң В§2.1 verified state table мһ‘м„ұ мқҳл¬ҙ вҖ” RequirementsPL self-write мӢң verify-before-trust к°Җ м •м°©. 4-claim вҶ” 1-row mandatory format.

#### A2-2 вҖ” Wave 1 (behavioral) + Wave 2 (mechanical) progression chain

ADR-040 Amendment 3 self-application Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 progression chain (Amendment 1 В§кІ°м • 6 м •н•©):

| Wave | scope | enforcement | carrier |
|---|---|---|---|
| Wave 1 (Amendment 2) | В§кІ°м • 1 (1-B) behavioral mandate | playbook В§3.17 + story-page-structure.md В§2.1 codification | CFP-1016 (ліё carrier) |
| Wave 2 (нӣ„мҶҚ CFP) | mechanical lint вҖ” `issue_origin: orchestrator_authored_followup` мӢң В§2.1 verified state table мЎҙмһ¬ + 4-column schema м •н•© lint | `scripts/check-story-section-issue-origin.sh` (deferred-followup, ADR-060 В§кІ°м • 5 лӘЁл“  мӢ к·ң entry warning мӢңмһ‘ к°•м ң м •н•©) | нӣ„мҶҚ CFP (лі„ carrier, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •) |
| Wave 3 (cross-repo, нӣ„мҲңмң„ ratchet) | RequirementsPL spawn prompt template (`mclayer/plugin-codeforge-requirements` вҖ” нҳ„ `plugins/codeforge-requirements/`, кө¬ repo мӮӯм ңлҗЁ 2026-06-12) explicit verify-before-trust mandate | cross-repo PR (canonical sibling sync, CFP-1002 precedent) | лі„лҸ„ canonical CFP carrier (wrapper-only Wave 1 мҡ°м„ , sibling sync нӣ„мҲңмң„ ratchet) |

Wave 2/3 = deferred-followup, ліё Amendment 2 frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` к°ұмӢ  0кұҙ (Wave 1 = behavioral mandate + template codification, mechanical lint мһҗмІҙлҠ” Wave 2 carrier). Amendment 1 мқҳ `corpus-claim-verify` + `cross-plugin-ownership-verify` 2 entry мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 2 scope (1-B) мҷҖ disjoint sub-decision.

#### A2-3 вҖ” scope_boundary (out-of-scope)

ліё Amendment 2 **нҸ¬н•Ё**: В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) verify scope мқҳ (1-B) Issue body authorship time лӘ…мӢңм Ғ codify + Wave 1 behavioral + template (a) + playbook (b).

ліё Amendment 2 **out-of-scope** (мң м§Җ/лі„ carrier):

- **(c) RequirementsPL spawn prompt template** mandate (canonical-side `mclayer/plugin-codeforge-requirements` repo) вҖ” cross-repo sibling sync лҸҷл°ҳ к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ, CFP-1002 precedent м •н•© (wrapper-only Story мҡ°м„ , cross-repo sibling sync нӣ„мҲңмң„ ratchet) вҶ’ лі„лҸ„ canonical CFP carrier.
- **Wave 2 mechanical lint** (`scripts/check-story-section-issue-origin.sh`) = нӣ„мҶҚ CFP carrier (deferred-followup, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •).
- ADR-073 frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` ліҖкІҪ = ADR-073 ліёл¬ё 0кұҙ ліҖкІҪ (cross-ref only вҖ” Amendment 2 к°Җ В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope нҷ•мһҘ лӘ…мӢң within ADR-082, ADR-073 ліёл¬ёмқҖ Wave 1 cross-repo state verify scope мң м§Җ).
- мӢ к·ң ADR м°Ҫм„Ө = Amendment only (ADR-RESERVATION мӢ к·ң row 0).

### Compatibility

- В§кІ°м • 1~8 + В§ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё + В§м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (corpus 4кұҙ вҶ’ 7кұҙ нҷ•мһҘ) + Amendment 1 м „л¶Җ мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 2 лҠ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope (1-B) лӘ…мӢң codify + corpus 4/5/6 м¶”к°Җ only.
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification вҖ” Amendment 2 = forbid scope нҷ•мһҘ (Orchestrator verify scope к°Җ cross-repo state assertion вҶ’ Issue body authorship time м¶”к°Җ) = ratchet-up к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ, `sunset_justification: "N/A вҖ” ratchet к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ"` (frontmatter amendments[].sunset_justification verbatim, Amendment 1 sunset_justification format лӢөмҠө). `is_transitional: false` мң м§Җ.
- ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•© (к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙл§Ң вҖ” м•Ҫнҷ” л°©н–Ҙ 0кұҙ).
- ADR-040 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 7.A schema м •н•© вҖ” `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` 2-entry мң м§Җ (Amendment 1 мқҳ corpus-claim-verify + cross-plugin-ownership-verify, Amendment 2 к°Җ Wave 2 deferred-followup мңјлЎң declare only, frontmatter к°ұмӢ  0).
- ADR-073 (Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify) = Wave 1 base scope мң м§Җ, Amendment 2 к°Җ ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope (1-B) лЎң codify (ADR-073 ліёл¬ё 0кұҙ ліҖкІҪ, cross-ref only).
- ADR-054 doc-only fast-path = ліё Amendment 2 carrier (CFP-1016) м ҒкІ© (ADR Amendment + template м¶”к°Җ + playbook м¶”к°Җ, src/tests л¬ҙліҖкІҪ 3-мЎ°кұҙ AND PASS, ADR-054 м •н•©).

### Related (Amendment 2 лҸҷл°ҳ)

- `templates/story-page-structure.md` вҖ” В§2.1 verified state table codification (mandatory when `issue_origin: orchestrator_authored_followup`) + `issue_origin` frontmatter field мӢ м„Ө
- `docs/orchestrator-playbook.md` вҖ” В§3.17 мӢ м„Ө (Orchestrator-authored Issue body pre-publish verify mandate)
- `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/{stories,change-plans}/CFP-1016*` вҖ” Amendment 2 carrier Story (doc-only fast-path лӢЁмқј PR pair)
- нӣ„мҶҚ carrier (Wave 2 mechanical lint) = лі„лҸ„ CFP, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •
- нӣ„мҶҚ canonical carrier (Wave 3 cross-repo) = лі„лҸ„ CFP, RequirementsPL spawn prompt template mandate

## Amendment 3 вҖ” ADR-085 cross-ref (disjoint complement вҖ” verify axis вҶ” coordination axis, CFP-1041, 2026-05-20 KST)

### м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

ADR-082 base + Amendment 1 + Amendment 2 лҠ” лӘЁл‘җ **verify axis** (internal lane agent self-write мқҳ write-time semantic truth verify вҖ” В§9 evidence / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration / Orchestrator-authored Issue body authorship мҳҒм—ӯ). к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ **ліөмҲҳ Claude Code session мқҙ лҸҷмқј repository / Story / branch лҸҷмӢң мһ‘м—… мӢң ownership кІ°м • / л¶„лӢҙ / handoff** мҳҒм—ӯмқҖ ADR-082 scope мҷё вҖ” verify axis м•„лӢҢ coordination axis (pre-hoc cross-session). 8 parallel race incidents single session lineage (CFP-953/946/949/932/954/991/967/1014, 2026-05-18 ~ 2026-05-19 KST) к°Җ ADR-045 В§D-9 cross_story_pattern_adr_trigger pattern_count вүҘ 8 reach escalation_action `adr_draft_emitted` мӮ°л¬ј вҖ” verify axis (ADR-073/070/082/045 В§D) к°Җ лӘЁл‘җ м¶©мЎұлҗҳм–ҙлҸ„ coordination axis л¶Җмһ¬ мӢң parallel race м°ЁлӢЁ л¶Ҳк°Җ.

### Amendment

ADR-085 (Multi-session collaboration protocol) мӢ м„ӨлЎң н•ҙлӢ№ gap мқ„ disjoint complement coordination axis layer лЎң codify. ADR-082 вҶ” ADR-085 = **disjoint complement кҙҖкі„** (verify axis вҶ” coordination axis):

- **ADR-082 (ліё ADR)** = internal lane agent self-write н•ңм • (В§9 evidence / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration / Issue body authorship write-time semantic truth verify, **verify axis**)
- **ADR-085** = ліөмҲҳ Claude Code session лҸҷмӢң мһ‘м—… мӢң ownership кІ°м • / л¶„лӢҙ / handoff (**coordination axis**, pre-hoc cross-session)

л‘җ layer лҠ” **axis мһҗмІҙк°Җ лӢӨлҰ„** вҖ” verify axis к°Җ м¶©мЎұлҗҳм–ҙлҸ„ coordination axis л¶Җмһ¬ мӢң parallel race л°ңмғқ, coordination axis кІ°м • нӣ„м—җлҸ„ verify axis лҜёмҲҳн–ү мӢң false claim. л‘ҳ лӢӨ н•„мҡ”н•ң orthogonal layer.

#### Amendment 3 вҖ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer disjoint 5-layer н‘ң anchor (ADR-085 В§кІ°м • 1 лӢөмҠө base)

ліё ADR В§кІ°м • 1 layer disjoint **4-layer** н‘ң (ADR-073 / ADR-070 / ADR-082 / ADR-045 В§D) к°Җ ADR-085 В§кІ°м • 1 layer disjoint **5-layer** н‘ңмқҳ **verbatim лӢөмҠө base** вҖ” ADR-085 В§ кІ°м • 1 5-layer н‘ң = ліё ADR В§кІ°м • 1 4-layer н‘ң + 5лІҲм§ё row "Multi-session coordination (ADR-085, coordination axis)" мӢ м„Ө.

| layer | ADR | scope | axis |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | ADR-073 | Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify | verify (post-hoc cross-repo) |
| 2 | ADR-070 | Codex external worker output verify | verify (post-hoc external) |
| 3 | **ADR-082 (ліё ADR)** | Internal lane agent В§9 evidence / Phase 0 mapping / corpus enumeration write-time verify | verify (write-time internal) |
| 4 | ADR-045 В§D | PMOAgent retro corpus enumeration cross-Story pattern_count escalation | verify (cross-Story pattern aggregator) |
| 5 | ADR-085 | Multi-session ownership / л¶„лӢҙ / handoff coordination | **coordination (pre-hoc cross-session)** |

ліё ADR (ADR-082) = row 3 = verify axis (write-time internal). ADR-085 = row 5 = coordination axis (axis disjoint).

#### Amendment 3 вҖ” Cross-ref-only (ліёл¬ё 0кұҙ ліҖкІҪ invariant)

ліё Amendment 3 мқҖ **cross-ref-only** вҖ” ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1-8 + Amendment 1-2 + ліёл¬ё В§кІ°м • / mechanism мқҳлҜё ліҖкІҪ 0. ADR-085 В§кІ°м • 1 5-layer н‘ң anchor к°Җ ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 4-layer н‘ң verbatim лӢөмҠө + 5лІҲм§ё row мӢ м„Ө (ADR-082 ліёл¬ё 0кұҙ ліҖкІҪ invariant ліҙмЎҙ). ADR-082 Amendment 1 ADR-073 cross-ref pattern verbatim лӢөмҠө (disjoint ліҙмҷ„ кҙҖкі„ cross-ref-only Amendment, mechanism scope м№ЁлІ” 0).

### Compatibility

- В§кІ°м • 1~8 + В§ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё + В§м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (corpus 4кұҙ) + Amendment 1 + Amendment 2 м „л¶Җ мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 3 мқҖ ADR-085 cross-ref ліҙмҷ„ кҙҖкі„ (disjoint complement) лӘ…мӢң only.
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification вҖ” Amendment 3 = cross-ref-only (disjoint complement лӘ…мӢң) = ratchet-up к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ, `sunset_justification: null` (forbid scope м¶•мҶҢ м•„лӢҳ). `is_transitional: false` мң м§Җ.
- ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•© (к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙл§Ң вҖ” м•Ҫнҷ” л°©н–Ҙ 0кұҙ).
- ADR-040 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 7.A schema м •н•© вҖ” `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` 2-entry мң м§Җ (Amendment 1 мқҳ corpus-claim-verify + cross-plugin-ownership-verify, Amendment 3 frontmatter к°ұмӢ  0).
- ADR-073 (Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify) = Wave 1 base + Amendment 1-2 + Amendment 4 (ADR-085 cross-ref) лҸҷнҳ• precedent вҖ” Amendment 4 cross-ref-only pattern лҸҷмқј.

### Related (Amendment 3 лҸҷл°ҳ)

- `docs/adr/ADR-085-multi-session-collaboration-protocol.md` вҖ” disjoint complement (verify axis вҶ” coordination axis). ADR-085 В§кІ°м • 1 5-layer н‘ң anchor к°Җ ліё ADR В§кІ°м • 1 4-layer н‘ң verbatim лӢөмҠө base.
- `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/stories/CFP-1041.md` вҖ” Amendment 3 carrier Story
- `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/change-plans/CFP-1041-multi-session-collaboration-protocol.md` вҖ” Change Plan (Phase 1 carrier)
- нӣ„мҶҚ carrier (Wave 2 mechanical wire вҖ” active_sessions[] presence lint + lane-entry sentinel subprocess invoke) = лі„ sub-CFP, ADR-085 В§кІ°м • 8 deferred-followup carrier

## Amendment 4 вҖ” ADR-RESERVATION `amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree cross-ref (Amendment id race convention нҳ•мӢқнҷ”, CFP-1058, 2026-05-20 KST)

### м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

CFP-1041 (Multi-session collaboration protocol Story-1) м§„н–ү мӨ‘ CFP-689 (ADR-073 Amendment 3 worktree-first self-ownership verify) мҷҖ Amendment id race л°ңмғқ. CFP-1041 carrier к°Җ ADR-082 Amendment 3 default мқёмҡ© вҶ’ CFP-689 к°Җ лҸҷмқј Amendment 3 slot м җмң  вҶ’ CFP-1041 inline renumber нӣ„ Amendment 4 лЎң м§„мһ…. **race-winner-takes-it informal convention** м Ғмҡ© (Amendment лІҲнҳё reservation field л¶Җмһ¬) вҖ” formalize мқҳл¬ҙ.

ADR-RESERVATION к°Җ **ADR number** reservation field ліҙмң н•ҳлӮҳ **Amendment id** reservation field л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ informal convention л§Ң м Ғмҡ©. Amendment id race recurrence м°ЁлӢЁ мң„н•ҙ schema codify мқҳл¬ҙ.

### Amendment

ADR-RESERVATION schema `amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree мӢ м„Ө (CFP-1058 carrier) cross-ref. ліё Amendment 4 = ADR-082 ліёл¬ё мҳҒм—ӯ ліҖкІҪ 0 (cross-ref-only Amendment).

#### Amendment 4 вҖ” `amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree schema codify cross-ref

```yaml
amendments_reserved:
  - adr_number: <N>
    amendment_id: <M>
    reserved_by_cfp: <CFP-NNN>
    reservation_date: <YYYY-MM-DD KST>
    status: reserved | active | superseded
```

к°Ғ ADR Amendment мӢ м„Ө мқҳлҸ„ мӢң ArchitectAgent (chief author) к°Җ commit time м җмң  м§Ғм „ `amendments_reserved[]` row append вҶ’ race-winner-takes-it мҳҒм—ӯ reservation-then-commit мҳҒм—ӯмңјлЎң м „нҷҳ. ліё schema = ADR-RESERVATION мқҳ кё°мЎҙ ADR number reservation field мҳҶ sibling sub-tree (file мӢ м„Ө 0, лӢЁмқј SSOT м •н•©).

#### Amendment 4 вҖ” Cross-ref-only (ліёл¬ё 0кұҙ ліҖкІҪ invariant)

ліё Amendment 4 лҠ” **cross-ref-only** вҖ” ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1-8 + Amendment 1-3 ліёл¬ё мқҳлҜё ліҖкІҪ 0. ADR-RESERVATION schema нҷ•мһҘ (`amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree мӢ м„Ө) л§Ң cross-ref. ADR-082 Amendment 3 ADR-085 cross-ref-only pattern + ADR-073 Amendment 4 cross-ref-only pattern verbatim лӢөмҠө (disjoint ліҙмҷ„ кҙҖкі„ cross-ref-only Amendment, mechanism scope м№ЁлІ” 0).

### Compatibility

- В§кІ°м • 1~8 + В§ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё + В§м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (corpus 4кұҙ) + Amendment 1 + Amendment 2 + Amendment 3 м „л¶Җ мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 4 лҠ” ADR-RESERVATION `amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree cross-ref only.
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification вҖ” Amendment 4 = cross-ref-only (schema codify к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ) = ratchet-up, `sunset_justification: null` (forbid scope м¶•мҶҢ м•„лӢҳ). `is_transitional: false` мң м§Җ.
- ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•© (к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙл§Ң вҖ” м•Ҫнҷ” л°©н–Ҙ 0кұҙ).
- ADR-040 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 7.A schema м •н•© вҖ” `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` 2-entry мң м§Җ (Amendment 1 мқҳ corpus-claim-verify + cross-plugin-ownership-verify, Amendment 4 frontmatter к°ұмӢ  0).
- ADR-082 Amendment 6+7 В§кІ°м • 9 forcing function м •н•© вҖ” `amendments_reserved[]` schema codify = Amendment id pre-reservation enables Wave 2 mechanical lint `amendment-number-frontmatter-verify` мқҳ reservation-aware нӣ„мҶҚ нҷ•мһҘ к°ҖлҠҘ (Wave N future carrier).

### Related (Amendment 4 лҸҷл°ҳ)

- `docs/adr/ADR-RESERVATION.md` вҖ” `amendments_reserved[]` sub-tree schema мӢ м„Ө (Amendment id race convention нҳ•мӢқнҷ”)
- `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/stories/CFP-1058.md` вҖ” Amendment 4 carrier Story
- `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/wrapper/change-plans/CFP-1058-adr-reservation-amendment-id.md` вҖ” Change Plan
- CFP-689 PR вҖ” Amendment id race winner evidence (race-winner-takes-it convention precedent)
- нӣ„мҶҚ carrier (Wave 2 mechanical lint вҖ” `amendments_reserved[]` presence + reservation-aware Check (a) нҷ•мһҘ) = лі„ sub-CFP, deferred-followup

---

## Amendment 5 вҖ” Lane PL spawn prompt user-utterance verbatim anchor (CFP-1110, 2026-05-20 KST)

### м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё

ліё Amendment 5 = **мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м§Ғк¶Ң minimal path мІ« м Ғмҡ©** (paradox-break first application). мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ directive 2026-05-20 KST verbatim:

> "м–ҙмЁҢл“  мӢңк°„мқҙ мҳӨлһҳкұёлҰ¬л“  л№„мҡ©мқҙ л§Һмқҙ лӮҳмҳӨл“  л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ м„ұлҠҘмқҙ м ңмқј мӨ‘мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ. к·јлҚ° мӢңк°„лҸ„ мҳӨлһҳкұёлҰ¬лҠ”лҚ° л Ҳмқёмқҙ м§ҖлӮ мҲҳлЎқ лӮҙк°Җ мҡ”кө¬н–ҲлҚҳ мҡ”кұҙмқҙ нқ©м–ҙм§Җкі  мқҙмғҒн•ң мһ‘м—…л§Ң мҲҳн–үн•ҳлҠ” кІғ к°ҷм•„м„ң к·ёл ҮлӢӨ."

ліём§Ҳ = **lane traversal fidelity loss** вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ л°ңнҷ” мӣҗл¬ёмқҙ lane нҶөкіјл§ҲлӢӨ мһ¬н•©м„ұлҗҳл©° weight к°Җ нқ¬м„қ, lane лӮҙл¶Җ invariant к°Җ к·ё мһҗлҰ¬лҘј м°Ём§Җн•ҳлҠ” нҳ„мғҒ. Researcher (general-purpose) + Codex лі‘л ¬ critical evaluation кІ°кіј:

- Researcher: codeforge dogfooding net 35% м •лӢ№нҷ” (verify-before-trust + Epic gate мҳҒм—ӯл§Ң), лӮҳлЁём§Җ 80% = self-burdening sunk cost cycle
- Codex: ROI indeterminate, л¶Җм • мӘҪ кё°мҡёкё°, confidence medium вҖ” denominator (consumer-protective fraction) мёЎм • л¶Җмһ¬
- мҲҳл ҙ: sunset asymmetry (мӢӨ retire 0кұҙ since codeforge м •мғҒ мҡҙмҳҒ м§„мһ…), self-referential dogfood paradox л§Ңм„ұнҷ”, mechanical layer к°Җ race м°ЁлӢЁ л¶Ҳк°Җ мһ…мҰқ

### pattern corpus лҲ„м Ғ evidence

| # | м¶ңмІҳ | нҢЁн„ҙ | count |
|---|---|---|---|
| 7a | CFP-722/801/792/810/819/825 | synthesizer-stale-reference (synthesis layer мӣҗліё drift) | 6 |
| 7b | CFP-698 | Researcher agent fact drift (12 occurrence м •м •) | 12 |
| 7c | CFP-758 | scope мһ¬нҷ•лҢҖ кёҲм§Җ invariant 6+ мң„м№ҳ л°•м ң вҶ’ scope drift л§Ңм„ұ evidence | 6+ |
| 7d | unverified-self-write-claim super-class (CFP-746/770/1000/1001/1002) | write-time semantic truth verify л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ ADR-082 carrier | 5 |
| 7e | CFP-906 | DesignReviewPL cross-PL false-negative (review к°Җ мӮ¬мӢӨкіј лӢӨлҘё кІ°лЎ ) | 1 |

PMOAgent ADR-045 В§D-9 м •лҹү мһ„кі„к°’: pattern_count **вүҘ 6** вү« threshold 2 вҶ’ Mandatory framing + escalation_action `escalate_user` вҶ’ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӢЁмқј super-class нҶөн•© кІ°м • (ліё Amendment 5 + paired ADR-071 Amendment 6).

### кө¬мЎ°м Ғ мӣҗмқё (3)

1. **Story В§1 мӣҗл¬ё вҶ’ В§2 Why / В§3 Design мһ¬н•©м„ұ мҶҗмӢӨ** вҖ” л§Ө lane PL spawn prompt м•Ҳ anchor к°Җ мһ¬н•©м„ұлҗң weight л§Ң нқҳлҹ¬к°„лӢӨ. мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мӣҗл¬ё verbatim мқҙ lane prompt м•Ҳ 1st-class anchor к°Җ м•„лӢҳ.
2. **codeforge-design lane fan-out л¶Ҳк· нҳ•** вҖ” chief + 5 deputy + 4-tuple sub-tuple = 10+ agent advocacy. 1 user мҡ”кө¬ vs 10+ deputy mandate мқҳ weight л№„лҢҖм№ӯ, deputy к°Җ мһҗкё° mandate мҳҒм—ӯ expansion л§Ң к°•нҷ” (cross-lane requirement traceability м•Ҫнҷ”).
3. **DialogFidelityAgent read-only** (ADR-071 В§кІ°м • 13) вҖ” `post_user_turn` / `pre_architectpl_synthesis` / `pre_fix_rootcause` 3-anchor м—җм„ң divergence кІҖм¶ңмқҖ к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳлӮҳ, lane мһ¬мӢӨн–ү к°•м ң лӘ»н•Ё (verifier мһҗмІҙк°Җ binding м•Ҫн•Ё) вҖ” paired ADR-071 Amendment 6 к°Җ binding к°•нҷ” carrier.

### Amendment

#### A5-1 вҖ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) sub-scope (1-C) мӢ м„Ө

В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (ADR-073) Orchestrator cross-repo state / assumption verify мқҳ м Ғмҡ© лІ”мң„м—җ **Lane PL spawn prompt user-utterance verbatim anchor** лӘ…мӢңм Ғ codify:

| sub-scope | trigger | verify мқҳл¬ҙ |
|---|---|---|
| (1-A) lane spawn / cross-repo state assertion | lane м§„мһ… мӢң мҷёл¶Җ state лӢЁм • | `git fetch origin` + `git show origin/main:<path>` + `verified-via` annotation (Wave 1 = ADR-073) |
| (1-B) Orchestrator-authored Issue body claim | Orchestrator к°Җ retro time / brainstorm Phase 0 нӣ„мҶҚ / ADR amendment carrier reservation / pattern_count escalation forcing function мӮ°л¬јлЎң Issue body лҘј author н•  л•Ң | Issue body м•Ҳ лӘЁл“  `claim` source direct verify нӣ„ author (Wave 1 = Amendment 2) |
| **(1-C) Orchestrator-authored lane PL spawn prompt** | **Orchestrator к°Җ lane PL agent (RequirementsPLAgent / ArchitectPLAgent / DesignReviewPLAgent / DeveloperPLAgent / CodeReviewPLAgent / SecurityTestPLAgent л“ұ) лҘј spawn н•  л•Ң** | **spawn prompt мІ« мӨ„м—җ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ л°ңнҷ” мӣҗл¬ё verbatim block мқҳл¬ҙ л¶Җм°© вҖ” мһ¬н•©м„ұ / мҡ”м•Ҫ / paraphrase / н•©м„ұл¬ё weight м Ғмҡ© кёҲм§Җ. lane PL мқҳ self-write deliverable мқҖ ліё verbatim anchor лҘј source of truth лЎң referencing мқҳл¬ҙ. Amendment 5 мӢ м„Ө** |

verbatim block нҳ•мӢқ:

```
[USER-UTTERANCE-VERBATIM]
> <мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мӣҗл¬ё л°ңнҷ” verbatim, н•ң кёҖмһҗ ліҖнҳ• м—ҶмқҢ>
[/USER-UTTERANCE-VERBATIM]
```

ліөмҲҳ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ л°ңнҷ” turn мӢң multiple verbatim block лҳҗлҠ” chronological list нҳ•нғң н—Ҳмҡ©. Story В§1 к°Җ мқҙлҜё verbatim ліҙмЎҙ SSOT мқҙлҜҖлЎң spawn prompt = Story В§1 л°ңнҷ” chunk м§Ғм ‘ quote (`git show origin/main:docs/stories/<KEY>.md` лҳҗлҠ” `mclayer/codeforge-internal-docs/<plugin>/stories/<KEY>.md` м§Ғм ‘ read-and-embed).

#### A5-2 вҖ” Citation вү  Reframing кІҪкі„

ліё Amendment 5 мқҳ verbatim мқҳл¬ҙлҠ” **мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мӣҗл¬ё** н•ңм •. Lane PL мқҙ spawn prompt м•Ҳм—җм„ң мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мӣҗл¬ё verbatim block мң„ / м•„лһҳ / мҳҶм—җ Orchestrator мһҗмӢ мқҳ н•©м„ұ м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (Story В§2 Why / В§3 Design мҡ”м•Ҫ / cross-lane reference) лҘј м¶”к°Җн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҖ н—Ҳмҡ© (В§кІ°м • 4 citation вү  assertion кІҪкі„ м •н•©). лӢЁ:

- verbatim block м•Ҳ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мӣҗл¬ё мһҗмІҙ modify = мң„л°ҳ (paraphrase кёҲм§Җ)
- verbatim block л¶Җмһ¬ = мң„л°ҳ (anchor м—Ҷмқҙ н•©м„ұл¬ёл§Ң м „лӢ¬)
- verbatim block мң„м№ҳ = spawn prompt **мІ« мӨ„** (anchor priority ліҙмЎҙ, weight нқ¬м„қ м°ЁлӢЁ)

#### A5-3 вҖ” Wave 1 (behavioral) + Wave 2 (mechanical) progression chain

ADR-040 Amendment 3 self-application Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 progression chain (Amendment 1 В§кІ°м • 6 / Amendment 2 В§A2-2 м •н•©):

| Wave | scope | enforcement | carrier |
|---|---|---|---|
| Wave 1 (Amendment 5) | В§кІ°м • 1 (1-C) behavioral mandate | playbook В§3.18 мӢ м„Ө (Orchestrator self-discipline вҖ” lane PL spawn prompt verbatim anchor мқҳл¬ҙ) + ADR-071 Amendment 6 paired (back-translation gate binding) | CFP-1110 (ліё carrier) |
| Wave 2 (нӣ„мҶҚ CFP) | mechanical lint вҖ” `Agent` tool spawn prompt м•Ҳ `[USER-UTTERANCE-VERBATIM]` block presence + Story В§1 л°ңнҷ” chunk match check | `scripts/check-spawn-prompt-user-utterance-anchor.sh` (deferred-followup, ADR-060 В§кІ°м • 5 лӘЁл“  мӢ к·ң entry warning мӢңмһ‘ к°•м ң м •н•©) | нӣ„мҶҚ CFP (лі„ carrier, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •) |

Wave 2 = deferred-followup, ліё Amendment 5 frontmatter `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` к°ұмӢ  0кұҙ (Wave 1 = behavioral mandate + playbook codification, mechanical lint мһҗмІҙлҠ” Wave 2 carrier). Amendment 1 мқҳ `corpus-claim-verify` + `cross-plugin-ownership-verify` 2 entry мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 5 scope (1-C) мҷҖ disjoint sub-decision.

#### A5-4 вҖ” scope_boundary (out-of-scope)

ліё Amendment 5 **нҸ¬н•Ё**: В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) sub-scope (1-C) Lane PL spawn prompt user-utterance verbatim anchor лӘ…мӢңм Ғ codify + Wave 1 behavioral + playbook В§3.18 мӢ м„Ө.

ліё Amendment 5 **out-of-scope** (мң м§Җ / лі„ carrier):

- **codeforge-design lane fan-out м¶•мҶҢ** (chief + 5 deputy + 4-tuple = 10+ agent вҶ’ н•өмӢ¬ 4-5 м¶•мҶҢ) вҖ” fidelity vs coverage trade, лі„лҸ„ к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ вҶ’ лі„лҸ„ CFP carrier (brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •).
- **Wave 2 mechanical lint** (`scripts/check-spawn-prompt-user-utterance-anchor.sh`) = нӣ„мҶҚ CFP carrier (deferred-followup).
- **back-translation gate binding** (lane return м§Ғнӣ„ PL reverse summary + DialogFidelityAgent divergence detection trigger lane мһ¬мӢӨн–ү) = paired ADR-071 Amendment 6 SSOT (ліё CFP-1110 лҸҷмқј carrier, ADR л¶„лҰ¬ вҖ” disjoint axis: ліё ADR = write-time input anchor / ADR-071 = return-time output gate).
- мӢ к·ң ADR м°Ҫм„Ө = Amendment only (ADR-RESERVATION мӢ к·ң row 0).

### Compatibility

- В§кІ°м • 1~8 + В§ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё + В§м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (corpus 4кұҙ вҶ’ 7кұҙ нҷ•мһҘ вҖ” 7a-e) + Amendment 1~4 м „л¶Җ мң м§Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment 5 лҠ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope (1-C) лӘ…мӢң codify + corpus 7a-e м¶”к°Җ only.
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification вҖ” Amendment 5 = forbid scope нҷ•мһҘ (Orchestrator verify scope к°Җ cross-repo state assertion + Issue body authorship вҶ’ Lane PL spawn prompt user-utterance verbatim anchor м¶”к°Җ) = ratchet-up к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ, `sunset_justification: "N/A вҖ” ratchet к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ"` (frontmatter amendments[].sunset_justification verbatim, Amendment 1/2 format лӢөмҠө). `is_transitional: false` мң м§Җ.
- ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•© (к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙл§Ң вҖ” м•Ҫнҷ” л°©н–Ҙ 0кұҙ).
- ADR-040 Amendment 3 В§кІ°м • 7.A schema м •н•© вҖ” `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` 2-entry мң м§Җ (Amendment 1 мқҳ corpus-claim-verify + cross-plugin-ownership-verify, Amendment 5 к°Җ Wave 2 deferred-followup мңјлЎң declare only, frontmatter к°ұмӢ  0).
- ADR-071 (Orchestrator-user dialog convergence) = paired Amendment 5 sibling carrier (back-translation gate binding, лҸҷмқј CFP-1110 carrier). л‘җ ADR axis disjoint complement (write-time input вҶ” return-time output).
- ADR-054 doc-only fast-path = ліё Amendment 5 carrier (CFP-1110) **л¶Җм ҒкІ©** (мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м§Ғк¶Ң minimal path = doc-only fast-path мҡ°нҡҢ вҖ” Story file 0, Phase 1+2 л¶„лҰ¬ 0, src ліҖкІҪмқҖ лӢЁ CLAUDE.md cross-ref + ADR Amendment 2мў… only). ADR-013 лӘ…мӢң мң„л°° (мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мҠ№мқё 2026-05-20 KST). closed-loop break мҷёл¶Җ кІ°м • мұ„л„җ вҖ” codeforge full flow м Ғмҡ© мӢң ліё нҸүк°Җ кІ°кіј (fidelity loss source) мһҗмІҙ мң„л°° paradox surface нҡҢн”ј.

### Related (Amendment 5 лҸҷл°ҳ)

- `docs/adr/ADR-071-orchestrator-user-dialog-convergence.md` вҖ” paired Amendment 5 (back-translation gate binding, lane return м§Ғнӣ„ verify, лҸҷмқј CFP-1110 carrier)
- `CLAUDE.md` вҖ” verify-before-trust 4-layer н‘ң лӢЁлқҪ ADR-082 Amendment 5 + ADR-071 Amendment 6 cross-ref 1-2мӨ„ (Orchestration к·ңм№ҷ В§"Lane м§„мһ… мӢң skill нҳём¶ң мқҳл¬ҙ" н‘ң м•Ҳ лҸҷл°ҳ)
- `mclayer/plugin-codeforge/issues/1110` вҖ” Amendment 5 carrier Issue (Story file 0 вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м§Ғк¶Ң minimal path)
- нӣ„мҶҚ carrier (Wave 2 mechanical lint вҖ” `scripts/check-spawn-prompt-user-utterance-anchor.sh` + workflow + evidence-checks-registry warning tier entry) = лі„ sub-CFP, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •
- нӣ„мҶҚ carrier (codeforge-design lane fan-out м¶•мҶҢ вҖ” к°Җм№ҳ нҢҗлӢЁ мҳҒм—ӯ) = лі„лҸ„ CFP, brainstorm лӢЁкі„ кІ°м •
