## Amendment 36 (2026-06-01 KST, CFP-1613) вҖ” sub-scope 1-Y `amendment_array_ordering_convention` (frontmatter amendments[] + amendment_log[] array ordering SSOT, hybrid: id ascending + reservation_date tie-break)

ліё Amendment лҠ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 (Orchestrator scope) sub-scope 1-Y мӢ м„Ө вҖ” ADR frontmatter `amendments[]` + `amendment_log[]` array мқҳ **row-append ordering convention SSOT**. ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 ratchet к°•нҷ” only (sub-scope 24вҶ’25 вҖ” convention codify, forbid scope м¶•мҶҢ 0кұҙ). MEDIUM Wave 1 declarative. лҸҷмқё = CFP-1601 retro F-DR-1601-2 P2 (paired sibling race CFP-1559 Amd 20 вҶ” CFP-1578 Amd 21 chronological-vs-id ordering ambiguity).

### Context

Amendment 30 (sub-scope 1-S) к°Җ ADR frontmatter **block convention** (single-block vs dual-block) мқ„ SSOT нҷ”н–ҲмңјлӮҳ, array **лӮҙл¶Җ row ordering convention** (м–ҙл–Ө мҲңм„ңлЎң row лҘј append н•ҳлҠ”к°Җ) мқҖ лҜёcodify мғҒнғңмҳҖлӢӨ. CFP-1601 retro F-DR-1601-2 P2 м—җм„ң paired-sibling race (CFP-1559 Amd 20 вҶ” CFP-1578 Amd 21) лҸҷмӢң reservation мӢң **chronological (reservation_date) vs id (amendment_id) ordering лӘЁнҳём„ұ** мқҙ surface вҖ” л‘җ CFP к°Җ лҸҷмӢңм—җ slot мқ„ мҳҲм•Ҫн•ҳл©ҙ append мҲңм„ңк°Җ мһ‘м„ұмһҗлі„лЎң к°Ҳл Ө frontmatter array к°Җ л№„кІ°м •м Ғ мҲңм„ңлЎң мһҗлһҖлӢӨ. dual-block-parity lint (sub-scope 1-Q/1-S, Amendment 28/30) лҠ” **set parity** (amendment_id м§‘н•© мқјм№ҳ) л§Ң кІҖмҰқн•ҳкі  **мҲңм„ң** лҠ” кІҖмҰқн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмңјлҜҖлЎң, мҲңм„ң л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳлҠ” lint-silent drift лЎң лҲ„м ҒлҗңлӢӨ.

anchor_id = `amendment_array_ordering_convention` / root_cause_class = `frontmatter-array-order-nondeterministic`. ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope 1-Y (disjoint from 1-A through 1-X вҖ” array ordering convention axis. 1-S block convention мқҳ sub-domain refinement: 1-S = "м–ҙл–Ө block мқ„ м“°лҠ”к°Җ" / 1-Y = "к·ё array м•Ҳ row лҘј м–ҙл–Ө мҲңм„ңлЎң м“°лҠ”к°Җ").

### В§A. Ordering convention SSOT (hybrid вҖ” id ascending + reservation_date tie-break)

`amendments[]` + `amendment_log[]` м–‘ array лӘЁл‘җ лӢӨмқҢ ordering мқҳл¬ҙ:

1. **Primary key вҖ” `amendment_id` ascending** (1, 2, 3, вҖҰ N). м–‘ block лӘЁл‘җ amendment_id мҳӨлҰ„м°ЁмҲңмңјлЎң row append. мӢ к·ң amendment = max amendment_id + 1 = array мөңн•ҳлӢЁ append (verify-before-trust source command = `grep -oE '^  - amendment_id: [0-9]+' <adr> | tail -1`, sub-scope 1-K precision rule м •н•©).
2. **Tie-break вҖ” `reservation_date` ascending** (paired-sibling-race н•ңм •). л‘җ CFP к°Җ лҸҷмқј мӢңм җ concurrent reservation мңјлЎң amendment_id м¶©лҸҢ мӢң, лЁјм Җ reserve н•ң (мқҙлҘё `reservation_date`) CFP к°Җ лӮ®мқҖ amendment_id м җмң . reslot л°ңмғқ мӢң В§B decision tree м Ғмҡ©.

Primary key (id ascending) к°Җ кұ°мқҳ лӘЁл“  кІҪмҡ°лҘј cover вҖ” reservation_date tie-break лҠ” concurrent collision (paired-sibling race) edge case н•ңм • л°ңлҸҷ.

### В§B. sub-scope letter вҶ” amendment_id mapping (NOT guaranteed synchronized)

sub-scope letter (1-A вҖҰ 1-Y) мҷҖ amendment_id (1 вҖҰ 36) лҠ” **лҸҷкё°нҷ” ліҙмһҘ м•Ҳ лҗЁ** вҖ” reslot race к°Җ л‘ҳмқ„ decouple н•ңлӢӨ.

**Evidence**: CFP-1684 к°Җ collision нӣ„ reslot лҗҳм–ҙ **Amd 31 / sub-scope 1-T** к°Җ лҗҗлӢӨ (CFP-1688 Amd 30 + sub-scope 1-S slot collision reslot вҖ” Amendment 31 body heading лӘ…мӢң). мҰү amendment_id 30вҶ”31 мӮ¬мқҙ sub-scope к°Җ 1-SвҶ”1-T лЎң нқҳл ҖмңјлӮҳ, н•ӯмғҒ `amendment_id N вҮ’ sub-scope = NлІҲм§ё letter` мӢқ м§Ғм ‘ л§Өн•‘мқҖ м„ұлҰҪ м•Ҳ н•ңлӢӨ (мҙҲкё° Amendment 1-7 мқҖ В§кІ°м • 6 л“ұ layer-level touch лЎң sub-scope letter лҜёл¶Җм—¬ вҖ” sub-scope letter лҠ” 1-A л¶Җн„° layer 1 Orchestrator scope sub-scope лҸ„мһ… нӣ„ sequential).

**мқҪлҠ” лІ• (mapping resolution)**: `amendment_log[]` entry к°Җ **both** field лҘј carry н•ңлӢӨ вҖ” `amendment_id` (м •мҲҳ slot) + `sub_scope` (мҳҲ `"1-W"`) + `ref` (мҳҲ `"## Amendment 34 + sub-scope 1-W row"`). mapping нҷ•мқё мӢң **amendment_log[] entry мқҳ `sub_scope` field к°Җ SSOT** (body heading мқҳ sub-scope н‘ңкё°лҠ” human-readable mirror). amendment_id вҶ” sub-scope лҸҷкё° к°Җм • кёҲм§Җ вҖ” entry field м§Ғм ‘ read мқҳл¬ҙ (verify-before-trust м •н•©).

### В§C. paired-sibling-race row-append decision tree

л‘җ CFP к°Җ concurrent н•ҳкІҢ amendment slot мқ„ мҳҲм•Ҫн•  л•Ң (paired-sibling race) row-append ordering ladder:

1. **к°Ғ CFP к°Җ spawn м§Ғм „ ADR-RESERVATION `amendments_reserved[]` row pre-append** (sub-scope 1-G strict pre-reservation mandate м •н•©) + spawn prompt `pre_reserved_amendment_slots: [{adr, amendment_id}]` field ліҙмң .
2. **collision лҜёл°ңмғқ (мҲңм°Ё reserve)**: лЁјм Җ reserve = лӮ®мқҖ amendment_id (max+1), лӮҳмӨ‘ reserve = к·ё лӢӨмқҢ (max+2). id ascending append. м •мғҒ case.
3. **collision л°ңмғқ (лҸҷмқј max+1 мқ„ л‘ҳмқҙ лҸҷмӢң claim)**: `reservation_date` tie-break вҖ” мқҙлҘё reservation_date CFP к°Җ max+1 м җмң , лҠҰмқҖ CFP лҠ” **reslot** (max+2 лЎң мқҙлҸҷ, мҰү reslotted entry к°Җ лҚ” лҶ’мқҖ id м җмң ). reslot лҗң CFP мқҳ sub-scope letter лҸ„ к·ём—җ л§һм¶° sequential мһ¬л°°м • (CFP-1684 вҶ’ Amd 31/1-T precedent).
4. **reservation_date лҸҷмқј (л¶„ лӢЁмң„ м¶©лҸҢ)**: carrier_story CFP лІҲнҳё ascending мқ„ final tie-break (лӮ®мқҖ CFP лІҲнҳё = лӮ®мқҖ amendment_id). deterministic ліҙмһҘ.

reslot нӣ„ commit м§Ғм „ **мһ¬verify мқҳл¬ҙ** (sub-scope 1-K Step 1 source command + sub-scope 1-V execution context): `git fetch origin main` + `grep -oE '^  - amendment_id: [0-9]+' <adr> | tail -1` actual next-slot мһ¬нҷ•мқё нӣ„ мөңмў… row append.

### В§D. Wave 1 declarative-only вҖ” Wave 2 лі„ sub-CFP carrier

`mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` мӢ к·ң entry 0 (convention codify вҖ” array мҲңм„ң lint лҠ” лі„ sub-CFP). Wave 2 carrier (CFP-1613-W2 reserved, мһ¬л°ң мӢң promote):
- `scripts/lib/check_adr_amendment_array_ordering.py` lint (amendment_id ascending кІҖмҰқ вҖ” dual-block-parity lint мқҳ set-parity лҘј order-parity лЎң нҷ•мһҘн•ҳлҠ” sub-domain)
- `templates/github-workflows/adr-amendment-array-ordering.yml` workflow (declarative anchor)
- bats fixture (id-ascending PASS / out-of-order WARNING / reslot tie-break)
- `docs/evidence-checks-registry.yaml` warning-tier entry + `hotfix-bypass:adr-amendment-array-ordering` family member

precedent 25-instance chain Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 split established. pattern_count вүҘ 2 м¶”к°Җ reach мӢң promote.

### В§E. Disjoint axis cross-ref

- ADR-082 sub-scope 1-S (CFP-1688, Amendment 30) вҖ” ADR frontmatter **block convention** SSOT (single-block vs dual-block, "м–ҙл–Ө block мқ„ м“°лҠ”к°Җ"). 1-Y = block лӮҙл¶Җ **row ordering** ("к·ё array row лҘј м–ҙл–Ө мҲңм„ңлЎң"). 1-Y лҠ” 1-S мқҳ sub-domain refinement (block convention вҶ’ row ordering convention).
- ADR-082 sub-scope 1-Q (CFP-1648, Amendment 28) вҖ” dual-block parity **set** кІҖмҰқ (amendment_id м§‘н•© мқјм№ҳ). 1-Y = **order** convention (set parity к°Җ verify м•Ҳ н•ҳлҠ” мҲңм„ң axis). lint мӢ м„Ө мӢң 1-Q sub-domain нҷ•мһҘ.
- ADR-082 sub-scope 1-G (CFP-1435, Amendment 17) вҖ” amendment-slot strict pre-reservation mandate. 1-Y В§C decision tree к°Җ 1-G pre-reservation мқ„ paired-race ordering ladder лЎң нҷ•мһҘ (pre-reservation нӣ„ collision мӢң reslot rule).
- ADR-082 sub-scope 1-K (CFP-1601, Amendment 22) вҖ” numeric claim source command precision. 1-Y next-slot кі„мӮ° (`grep вҖҰ | tail -1`) мқҙ 1-K source command rule м§Ғм ‘ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©.
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 вҖ” sunset_justification N/A ratchet-up (convention codify, scope м¶•мҶҢ 0). ADR-064 В§кІ°м • 7 (CFP-1149 Amendment 8) symmetric evidence-gated м •н•© (к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ, pattern evidence = CFP-1601 retro F-DR-1601-2 P2).

### В§F. META self-application (recursive dogfooding)

ліё Amendment 36 = sub-scope 1-Y мІ« м Ғмҡ© мӮ¬лЎҖ = self:
- ліё carrier к°Җ В§A id-ascending convention мқ„ ліё Amendment мһҗмӢ мқҳ row append м—җ м Ғмҡ© вҖ” `amendments[]` + `amendment_log[]` м–‘ block лӘЁл‘җ amendment_id 36 мқ„ max(35) + 1 = мөңн•ҳлӢЁ append (id ascending мӨҖмҲҳ).
- verify-before-trust: spawn м§Ғм „ `grep -oE '^  - amendment_id: [0-9]+' docs/adr/ADR-082-*.md | tail -1` actual = `amendment_id: 35` вҶ’ next-slot = 36 `[verified]` (sub-scope 1-K source command + 1-V execution context м •н•©).
- dual-block parity: ліё Amd 36 мқҳ amendments[] + amendment_log[] + body `## Amendment 36` 3-block parity ліҙмЎҙ (Amd 32 sub-scope 1-U dual-block gate self-application м •н•©).
- sub-scope letter = 1-Y (1-X = CFP-822 Amd 35 лӢӨмқҢ sequential вҖ” amendment_id 36 вҶ” sub-scope 1-Y лҸҷкё°, лӢЁ В§B м—җ л”°лқј лҸҷкё°лҠ” ліҙмһҘмқҙ м•„лӢҢ ліё case мқҳ мӮ¬мӢӨ).

### В§G. sunset_justification N/A м •лӢ№

is_transitional: false ліҙмЎҙ. Amd 36 = к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ only (sub-scope 24вҶ’25 ratchet нҷ•мһҘ + array ordering convention codify). ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification ratchet нҶөкіј (forbid scope нҷ•мһҘ, convention лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”). ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•©.

### В§H. Related

- CFP-1613 carrier Story (`<internal-docs>/plugin-codeforge/stories/CFP-1613.md`)
- CFP-1601 retro F-DR-1601-2 P2 вҖ” paired-sibling race ordering ambiguity origin (CFP-1559 Amd 20 вҶ” CFP-1578 Amd 21 chronological-vs-id)
- ADR-082 Amendment 30 (sub-scope 1-S) вҖ” block convention SSOT (ліё 1-Y мқҳ parent axis)
- ADR-082 Amendment 28 (sub-scope 1-Q) вҖ” dual-block parity set-check (order-check лҜёнҸ¬н•Ё вҖ” 1-Y к°Җ ліҙмҷ„)
- ADR-082 Amendment 17 (sub-scope 1-G) вҖ” amendment-slot strict pre-reservation (В§C decision tree base)
- reslot precedent: CFP-1684 вҶ’ Amd 31 / sub-scope 1-T (CFP-1688 Amd 30 / 1-S collision reslot)
- origin Issue: mclayer/plugin-codeforge#1613 (MEDIUM, Wave 1 declarative)
- ADR-054 В§кІ°м • 1 вҖ” doc-only fast-path м ҒкІ© (лӢЁмқј PR, scripts/tests л¬ҙліҖкІҪ)

## Amendment 37 (2026-06-20 KST, CFP-2383) вҖ” sub-scope 1-Z `spawn_prompt_fact_verify_wave2_wire_ssot` (sub-scope 1-L Amd 23 declaration-only вҶ’ Wave 2 mechanical wire SSOT: PR-body-proxy static presence-only lint binding)

ліё Amendment лҠ” В§кІ°м • 1 layer 1 sub-scope 1-Z мӢ м„Ө вҖ” sub-scope **1-L** (Amendment 23, CFP-1590) мқҳ Wave 1 declaration-only mandate лҘј **Wave 2 mechanical enforcement wire SSOT** лЎң codify н•ңлӢӨ. ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 ratchet к°•нҷ” only (sub-scope 25вҶ’26 вҖ” Wave 2 mechanical enforcement м¶”к°Җ, forbid scope м¶•мҶҢ 0кұҙ). warning-tier. Epic CFP-2380 S3. лҸҷмқё = CFP-2380 S1 deferred-followup-reconcile FLAG н•ҙмҶҢ (firsthand: `bash scripts/check-deferred-followup-reconcile.sh` мӢӨн–ү вҶ’ `spawn-prompt-fact-verify count=3/3 promotion_trigger=auto_blocking` [verified]).

> **Phase л¶„лҰ¬**: ліё Amendment (Phase 1) = ADR Amendment + `mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` entry status flip + binding л§Ң. мӢӨ lint script / workflow / discriminating test / `evidence-checks-registry.yaml` detect_commandВ·workflow мӢӨнҢҢмқј flip / `label-registry-v2` MINOR (`hotfix-bypass:spawn-prompt-fact-verify`) = **Phase 2 кө¬нҳ„ lane** мӮ°м¶ң (ліё Amendment м—җм„ң мһ‘м„ұ м•Ҳ н•Ё). S1(CFP-2381)/S2(CFP-2382) Phase 1+Phase 2 split precedent лӢөмҠө.

### Context

sub-scope 1-L (Amendment 23, CFP-1590) лҠ” "spawn prompt fact verify-before-trust mandate (upstream-inherited stale fact carrier super-class вҖ” workerвҶ’worker handoff)" лҘј **Wave 1 declaration-only** лЎң лҸ„мһ…н–ҲлӢӨ. `evidence-checks-registry.yaml` мқҳ `spawn-prompt-fact-verify` entry к°Җ к·ё anchor мқёлҚ°, `detect_command` мҷҖ `workflow` к°Җ мӢӨнҢҢмқј м—ҶлҠ” TBD мғҒнғң(`status: deferred-followup`)лЎң лӮЁм•„ н•ң лІҲлҸ„ mechanically wired лҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳлӢӨ. CFP-2380 S1 мқҙ мӢ м„Өн•ң deferred-followup-reconcile кІҢмқҙнҠёк°Җ мқҙ entry лҘј carrier_absent FLAG(count=3/3, auto_blocking)лЎң surface вҖ” ліё Amendment к°Җ к·ё FLAG лҘј н•ҙмҶҢн•ҳлҠ” Wave 2 mechanical wire SSOT.

anchor_id = `spawn_prompt_fact_verify_wave2_wire_ssot` / root_cause_class = `wave1-declaration-never-wired`. sub-scope 1-Z = disjoint from 1-A through 1-Y (1-L мқҳ mechanical enforcement wire axis вҖ” numeric-claim sub-scope 1-K(declaration)вҶ”1-N(Wave 2 wire) precedent лҸҷнҳ• pairing).

### В§A. м„Өкі„ кІ°м • 1 вҖ” wire л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ (3-source н•©м„ұ)

PR-body-proxy static presence-only lint = 3к°ң м„ лЎҖмқҳ н•©м„ұ:

1. **кө¬мЎ° / FP guard / exit code / test = S2 (`issue-body-claim-pre-screen`) лӢөмҠө** вҖ” line-by-line `in_fence` toggle masking + `strip_inline_code` + `PER_BLOCK_SCAN_CAP = 50` + `ANNOTATION_MARKER = "[verified-via:"` (м •м Ғ substring, м •к·ңмӢқ м•„лӢҳ) + exit `0=PASS / 1=FLAG / 2=SETUP`. Refactor м„ нғқм§Җ (b) мұ„нғқ (firsthand: `scripts/lib/check_issue_body_claim_pre_screen.py` L51/L54/L150-193 [verified]). м„ нғқм§Җ (a) 1-W нҶөм§ё ліөл¶ҷ = л¶Җм Ғн•© (exit 0 кі м • + window scan мқҙ S2 мқҳ FP к°ңм„  м—ӯн–ү), м„ нғқм§Җ (c) кіөнҶө lib м¶”м¶ң = мЎ°кё° (мқ‘м§‘л Ҙ лӮ®мқҢ вҖ” 3лІҲм§ё PATTERNS ліөліё л“ұмһҘ мӢң `fact_verify_patterns.py` кіөнҶө м¶”м¶ң мһ¬кІҖнҶ , ModuleArch consult; escalation marker ліҙмЎҙ).
2. **fact PATTERNS = мӮӯм ңлҗң 1-W source мқҳ C1-C5 мқҙмӢқ** вҖ” `c84fadf3:scripts/lib/check_orchestrator_spawn_prompt_fact_verify.py` мқҳ PATTERNS (firsthand: `git show c84fadf3:...` L55-90 [verified]): C1 counter `\b(\d{2,})\s+(entries|...)` / C2 version `\bv\d+\.\d+(?:\.\d+)?\b` / C3 SHA `\b[0-9a-f]{40}\b|PRE-SPAWN-ORIGIN-MAIN-SHA:` / C4 verify-result `sha256 PASS|byte-identical OK|MERGED|CLEAN|drift 0` / C5 file-existence `\S+\.(md|yml|...)\s+(мЎҙмһ¬|...)|line count:\d+`. **ReDoS-safe invariant**: C1-C5 nested quantifier 0 + scan cap 50 вҖ” мӢ к·ң regex м¶”к°Җ мӢң ReDoS invariant лӘ…л¬ё кІҖмҰқ мқҳл¬ҙ.
3. **trigger / event / body-source = `tier-downgrade-guard.yml` лӢөмҠө** вҖ” S2 лҠ” `on: issues` event(PR м•„лӢҳ)мқҙлҜҖлЎң PR-body-proxy canonical м„ лЎҖ л¶Җм Ғн•©. PR-event м„ лЎҖ = `tier-downgrade-guard.yml` (firsthand: `.github/workflows/tier-downgrade-guard.yml` [verified]): `on: pull_request: types:[opened, synchronize, reopened]` + `paths: [docs/...]` + `permissions: contents: read` + `env: <X>: ${{ github.event.pull_request.body }}` + `run: bash scripts/check-*.sh`.

annotation marker canonical = `[verified-via:` (S2 м •м Ғ substring нҳ•мӢқ 1к°ң кі м •). 1-L scope = workerвҶ’worker handoff, 4 sub-source (мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ л°ңнҷ” / sibling Issue body / sister PR commit message / лі„ carrier retro file).

### В§B. м„Өкі„ кІ°м • 2 вҖ” PR-body-proxy н•ңкі„ лӘ…мӢң (anti-theater)

PR body лҠ” workerвҶ’worker handoff spawn prompt мқҳ **proxy мқј лҝҗ мӢӨ spawn prompt к°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.** кІҖм¶ң лІ”мң„ = inherit fact к°Җ PR body м—җ transcribe лҗң кІҪмҡ°л§Ң вҖ” spawn prompt м§Ғм ‘ кІҖмӮ¬ м•„лӢҳ. мқҙ н•ңкі„лҘј лӘ…л¬ёнҷ”н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©ҙ surface theater (мӢӨм ңлЎң кІҖмӮ¬ м•Ҳ н•ҳлҠ” кІғмқ„ кІҖмӮ¬н•ҳлҠ” мІҷ) мң„н—ҳ. Phase 2 discriminating test к°Җ file-input кІҪлЎңлЎң surface мӢӨмЎҙмқ„ мҰқлӘ… мқҳл¬ҙ (S2 лҸҷнҳ•, mutation мғқмЎҙ 0 лӘ©н‘ң). м •м Ғ lint мқҙлҜҖлЎң В§8.5 stateful test N/A + Perf Baseline N/A (TestContractArch).

### В§C. м„Өкі„ кІ°м • 3 вҖ” 1-W orphan мІҳлҰ¬ (axis disjoint ліҙмЎҙ)

м ңкұ°лҗң sub-scope 1-W (Amendment 34, CFP-1842) мқҳ entry / mandate лҠ” **л¶Җнҷңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.** лӢЁмҲң 1-W нҢҢмқј ліөмӣҗ = ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 ratchet мң„л°° (de-bloat м ңкұ° мғҒнғң мң м§Җ). ліё wire лҠ” **1-L мқҳ мөңмҙҲ л°°м„ ** (1-L мқҖ declaration мқҙнӣ„ н•ң лІҲлҸ„ wired м•Ҳ лҗЁ). axis disjoint ліҙмЎҙ:

- **1-L** (CFP-1590) = worker self-write spawn prompt fact (workerвҶ’worker handoff) вҖ” ліё Amendment 37 мқҳ wire лҢҖмғҒ.
- **1-W** (CFP-1842) = Orchestrator-side spawn prompt fact (OrchestratorвҶ’subagent handoff) вҖ” лі„лҸ„ entry, лі„лҸ„ bypass label (firsthand: `hotfix-bypass:orchestrator-spawn-prompt-fact-verify` label-registry-v2.md L1942 л“ұлЎқ [verified]).

C1-C5 PATTERNS лҠ” 1-W source м—җм„ң мқҙмӢқн•ҳлҗҳ, scope / trigger / handoff axis лҠ” 1-L мҡ©мңјлЎң мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ (TestContractArch В§B message-assert TC = Phase 2 вҖ” 1-W мһ”мһ¬ м—Ҷмқҙ 1-L мҡ© мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ кІҖмҰқ).

### В§D. м„Өкі„ кІ°м • 4 вҖ” FP guard 4мў… EXEMPT

PR body лҸ„ markdown мқҙлҜҖлЎң S2 мқҳ false-positive guard 4мў… лӢөмҠө:

1. `in_fence` вҖ” fenced code block лӮҙл¶Җ (``` toggle) л©ҙм ң.
2. inline code-span вҖ” `` `...` `` (`strip_inline_code` masking) л©ҙм ң.
3. blockquote вҖ” `>` prefix н–ү л©ҙм ң.
4. SELF_SOURCE вҖ” fact мһҗмІҙмқҳ source м„ м–ё н–ү л©ҙм ң.

`window = 5` кІҪкі„ + empty input PASS + setup error exit 2 (S2 boundary лӢөмҠө).

### В§E. м„Өкі„ кІ°м • 5 вҖ” deferral лӘ…л¬ёнҷ” + #2166 мўҢн‘ң

ліё Story м—җм„ң **wire н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”** deferred entry 2кұҙ (status retain вҖ” ADR-082 ratchet мӮӯм ң л¶Ҳк°Җ):

- **retro-fact-verify-mandate** (Amendment 31 / sub-scope **1-T**, CFP-1684 вҖ” body heading к¶Ңмң„ [verified: `## Amendment 31 ... sub-scope (1-T) ... PMOAgent retro write-time verify-before-trust mandate (CFP-1684 ... CFP-1688 Amd 30/1-S slot collision reslot)`]; registry entry description мқҳ "Amendment 30/1-S" н‘ңкё°лҠ” reslot stale мһ”мһ¬ вҖ” body heading SSOT). deferral мӮ¬мң  = retro лҠ” cross-repo (`docs/retros` к°Җ internal-docs repo м—җ мҳҒмҶҚ вҶ’ wrapper CI surface 0 вҶ’ wrapper м—җм„ң lint н•ҳл©ҙ кұ°м§“ inventory мң„н—ҳ).
- **fix-loop-reverify-mandate** (Amendment 29 / sub-scope **1-R**, CFP-1683). deferral мӮ¬мң  = 3 field (`amendment_slot_revalidated` / `registry_version_revalidated` / `bypass_count_revalidated`) к°Җ fix-event-v1 schema м—җ лҜёмҳҒмҶҚ вҶ’ static lint н•ҳл Өл©ҙ schema MINOR bump м„ н–ү мқҳмЎҙ вҶ’ ліё Story scope мҙҲкіј.

**#2166 л¶Җл¶„ close**: ліё Amendment к°Җ 1-L (spawn-prompt-fact-verify) лҘј wire н•ЁмңјлЎңмҚЁ #2166 мқҳ н•ҙлӢ№ л¶Җл¶„ close. мһ”м—¬ мўҢн‘ң = (a) мҷёл¶Җм§ҖмӢқ `source:` annotation lint + (b) мҲҳм№ҳ мёЎм •л°©лІ• лӘ…кё° lint вҖ” мң„ 3 entry (1-L wire + 2 deferral) л°– мһ”м—¬ (лі„ carrier vs ліё Epic нӣ„мҶҚ Story нқЎмҲҳ кІ°м •мқҖ Orchestrator/PMO мўҢн‘ң).

### В§F. ліҙм•Ҳ / мҡҙмҳҒ м •н•©

- **В§7.4.5 env-isolation (P1)**: `pull_request` event (NOT `pull_request_target`) + `permissions: contents: read, pull-requests: read` (write 0, secret 0). PR body лҠ” env кІҪмң л§Ң (`run:` inline `${{ github.event.pull_request.body }}` ліҙк°„ кёҲм§Җ вҖ” shell injection м°ЁлӢЁ). мӮӯм ңлҗң 1-W workflow (`c84fadf3:.github/workflows/orchestrator-spawn-prompt-fact-verify.yml:27` inline-interpolation injection м•ҲнӢ°нҢЁн„ҙ + `GH_TOKEN` secret fetch) ліөм ң кёҲм§Җ вҖ” S2/tier-downgrade-guard мқҳ env-injection + mktemp + python file-input н‘ңмӨҖ лӢөмҠө.
- **В§11.6 idempotency PASS** вҖ” pure presence-scan (лҸҷмқј мһ…л Ҙ лҸҷмқј кІ°кіј), registry / label-registry write = 1нҡҢм„ұ declarative.
- **В§11.1-В§11.5 N/A** вҖ” governance document schema (append-only ratchet м§Җл°°, ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 6 / ADR-008 В§кІ°м • 2 / ADR-010 В§кІ°м • 3), лҚ°мқҙн„° schema м•„лӢҳ.
- **В§7.3 auth / В§7.5 лҜјк°җлҚ°мқҙн„° N/A** вҖ” мқёмҰқ мЈјмІҙ 0 / secret 0 / мһ…л Ҙ = repo-visible PR body.
- **ліҙм•Ҳ нҶөм ң мӢ лў° кёҲм§Җ (T5 мҲҳмҡ©)**: `[verified-via:` мң„мЎ°лЎң мҡ°нҡҢ = presence-only lint ліём§Ҳм Ғ н•ңкі„. warning-tier advisory лқј ліҙм•Ҳ кІҢмқҙнҠё м•„лӢҳ. blocking мҠ№кІ© мӢң мң„мЎ° false-PASS к°Җ кө¬мЎ°м Ғ к°ҖлҠҘ вҶ’ "ліҙм•Ҳ нҶөм ңлЎң мӢ лў° кёҲм§Җ" (blocking мҠ№кІ© = лі„лҸ„ follow-up CFP MUST, pattern_count >= 5 мһ¬л°ң trigger).
- **detect_command лӢЁмҲңнҳ• мң м§Җ** вҖ” `bash scripts/check-spawn-prompt-fact-verify.sh` (м¶”к°Җ мқёмһҗ м—Ҷмқҙ, resolver shell-operator нҡҢн”ј). FLAG н•ҙмҶҢ л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳ = detect_command + workflow мӢӨнҢҢмқј мӢӨмЎҙ вҶ’ carrier_absent False вҶ’ FLAG мҶҢл©ё (Phase 2).

### В§G. Wave 2 mechanical wire мӮ°м¶ңл¬ј (Phase 2 лі„ sub-CFP / кө¬нҳ„ lane)

`mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` `spawn-prompt-fact-verify` entry status flip = ліё Phase 1 binding (S1 F1 көҗнӣҲ вҖ” мӢ к·ң lint carrier л©ҙ binding мқҳл¬ҙ). Phase 2 actual wire (Epic CFP-2380 S3 Phase 2 кө¬нҳ„ lane):

- `scripts/lib/check_spawn_prompt_fact_verify.py` (Python SSOT per ADR-061 вҖ” S2 кө¬мЎ° + C1-C5 PATTERNS мқҙмӢқ)
- `scripts/check-spawn-prompt-fact-verify.sh` (bash thin wrapper вҖ” envвҶ’mktempвҶ’python file-input, trap cleanup)
- `.github/workflows/spawn-prompt-fact-verify.yml` (**single-root** вҖ” `templates/github-workflows/` лҜёмӮ¬мҡ© firsthand нҷ•мқё [verified: S2 лҸ„ single-root]; CONSUMER_ONLY_WORKFLOWS / invariant-check parity л¶Ҳмҡ”. `pull_request` trigger + paths filter + permissions contents:read,pull-requests:read + env-injection)
- `scripts/test-check-spawn-prompt-fact-verify.sh` (discriminating test вҖ” S2 лҸҷнҳ•, fact categoryлі„ RED/GREEN мҢҚ + FP guard 4мў… + PER_BLOCK_SCAN_CAP=50 + window=5 кІҪкі„ + empty PASS + setup exit2 + В§B 1-W-мһ”мһ¬ message-assert + В§C fenced л№ҲмӨ„ fragmentation FP кІҪкі„)
- `docs/evidence-checks-registry.yaml` `spawn-prompt-fact-verify` detect_commandВ·workflow мӢӨнҢҢмқј flip + status `deferred-followup`вҶ’`active` (warning-tier)
- `label-registry-v2` MINOR вҖ” `hotfix-bypass:spawn-prompt-fact-verify` (1-L) family member м¶”к°Җ (вү  1-W `hotfix-bypass:orchestrator-spawn-prompt-fact-verify` вҖ” name м¶©лҸҢ нҡҢн”ј, primary-key disjoint) + MANIFEST.yaml version ratchet. kind:registry sibling sync л©ҙм ң (ADR-010 В§кІ°м • 2). plugin.json bump 0 = marketplace_sync_declared: false (mirrored field ліҖкІҪ 0).

precedent 26-instance Wave 1вҶ’Wave 2 split chain established + S2 (Amendment 20 CFP-1559 вҶ’ CFP-2382) лҸҷнҳ• м§Ғм „ precedent.

### В§H. Disjoint axis cross-ref

- ADR-082 sub-scope **1-L** (CFP-1590, Amendment 23) вҖ” ліё 1-Z мқҳ declaration parent (1-L = mandate м •мқҳ, 1-Z = к·ё Wave 2 mechanical enforcement wire SSOT). numeric-claim 1-K(declaration)вҶ”1-N(Wave 2 wire) precedent лҸҷнҳ• pairing.
- ADR-082 sub-scope **1-W** (CFP-1842, Amendment 34) вҖ” OrchestratorвҶ’subagent axis (de-bloat м ңкұ° мң м§Җ, ліөмӣҗ кёҲм§Җ). ліё 1-Z к°Җ к·ё C1-C5 PATTERNS л§Ң мқҙмӢқ (handoff axis мһ¬мһ‘м„ұ, л¶Җнҷң м•„лӢҳ).
- ADR-082 sub-scope **1-K/1-N** (CFP-1601/CFP-1612, Amendment 22/25) вҖ” numeric-claim declarationвҶ’Wave 2 wire precedent лӢөмҠө (ліё 1-Z к°Җ лҸҷнҳ• pairing).
- ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 15 (Amendment 20, CFP-1559 вҖ” `issue-body-claim-pre-screen`) вҖ” S2, ліё 1-Z мқҳ кө¬мЎ°/FP guard/exit/test лӢөмҠө base (м§Ғм „ лҸҷнҳ• precedent CFP-2382).
- ADR-060 В§кІ°м • 5 вҖ” warning mode first wire (presence-only, blocking мҠ№кІ© лі„лҸ„ CFP).
- ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 вҖ” sunset_justification N/A ratchet-up (Wave 2 enforcement м¶”к°Җ, scope м¶•мҶҢ 0). ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•©.
- ADR-054 В§кІ°м • 1 вҖ” Phase 1 doc-only fast-path м ҒкІ© (лӢЁмқј PR, scripts/tests л¬ҙліҖкІҪ вҖ” change-plan л©ҙм ң). firsthand precedent: `ls docs/change-plans/ | grep -i 238x` вҶ’ 0кұҙ (CFP-2381/CFP-2382 change-plan лҜёмһ‘м„ұ [verified]).
- paired sibling ADR-073 Amendment дёҚиҰҒ (sub-scope 1-Z = 1-L mechanical wire complement, workerвҶ’worker axis вү  Orchestrator verify-before-assert axis вҖ” 1-N/1-P precedent лӢөмҠө).

### В§I. META self-application (recursive dogfooding)

ліё Amendment 37 = sub-scope 1-Z мІ« м Ғмҡ© мӮ¬лЎҖ = self:

- id ascending convention (В§A Amd 36 1-Y) м Ғмҡ© вҖ” `amendments[]` + `amendment_log[]` м–‘ block лӘЁл‘җ amendment_id 37 мқ„ max(36) + 1 = мөңн•ҳлӢЁ append. source command verify `grep -oE '^  - amendment_id: [0-9]+' archive/adr/ADR-082-write-time-self-write-verification-mandate.md | tail -1` actual = `amendment_id: 36` (Amd 36 CFP-1613 м җмң ) вҶ’ м •нҷ• next-slot for CFP-2383 = 37 [verified].
- sub-scope letter = 1-Z (1-Y = CFP-1613 Amd 36 лӢӨмқҢ sequential вҖ” amendment_id 37 вҶ” sub-scope 1-Z, В§B(Amd 36) м—җ л”°лқј лҸҷкё°лҠ” ліҙмһҘмқҙ м•„лӢҢ ліё case мқҳ мӮ¬мӢӨ).
- dual-block parity: ліё Amd 37 мқҳ amendments[] + amendment_log[] + body `## Amendment 37` 3-block parity ліҙмЎҙ (Amd 32 sub-scope 1-U dual-block gate self-application м •н•©).
- ліё carrier мһҗмІҙк°Җ sub-scope 1-L (spawn prompt fact verify) мқҳ inherit-fact verify лҘј dogfood вҖ” ліё Amendment мқҳ лӘЁл“  мҲҳм№ҳ лӢЁм–ё (amendment_id 36/37 В· label-registry v2.97 В· FLAG 2кұҙ В· C1-C5 В· S1/S2 precedent) firsthand verify нӣ„ `[verified]` н‘ңкё° (м¶”м • lock-in 0).

### В§J. sunset_justification N/A м •лӢ№

is_transitional: false ліҙмЎҙ. Amd 37 = к°•нҷ” л°©н–Ҙ only (sub-scope 25вҶ’26 ratchet нҷ•мһҘ + 1-L Wave 2 mechanical enforcement wire codify). ADR-058 В§кІ°м • 5 sunset_justification ratchet нҶөкіј (forbid scope нҷ•мһҘ, enforcement м¶”к°Җ). ADR-064 В§self-application top-down ratchet м •н•©.

## Amendment 38 (2026-07-13 KST, CFP-2646) вҖ” В§кІ°м • 16 мӢ м„Ө `resource_safety_claim_proof_presence` (governance/ліҙм•Ҳ tooling docstringВ·мЈјм„қВ·мӣҢнҒ¬н”ҢлЎң YAML мЈјм„қмқҳ resource-safety/DoS-guard м•Ҳм „м„ұ-claim вҶ’ paired proof-reference OR honest-ceiling presence write-time м •м§Ғ discipline вҖ” write-time verify super-class 3лІҲм§ё presence-lint carrier)

> **honesty-ceiling мһҗкё°м Ғмҡ© м„ м–ё (ліё Amendment м „мІҙ мғҒмҶҚ вҖ” ADR-151 В§кІ°м •7)**: ліё Amendment мқҙ мӢ м„Өн•ҳлҠ” disciplineВ·lint мқҖ м•Ҳм „м„ұ-claim мқҙ **мҰқкұ°лҘј лҸҷл°ҳн•ҳлҠ”м§Җ(presence)** л§Ң кІҖмӮ¬н•ңлӢӨ. claim мқҳ **м°ёлҗЁ(truth)** мқҖ м •м Ғ лҸ„кө¬лЎң мҰқлӘ… л¶Ҳк°Җ вҖ” ліё Amendment мқҖ over-claim мқ„ "лҙүмқё/мҷ„м „л°©м§Җ" н•ҳм§Җ **м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ**. lint мқҖ claim-without-any-proof-link лҘј **мһ‘м„ұ мӢңм җм—җ мўҢн–Ҙ л…ём¶ң**н•  лҝҗмқҙлӢӨ. `presence вү  truth`. detection(ліҙм•Ҳн…ҢмҠӨнҠё execution-backed probe) мЎҙм№ҳ.

### В§A. м»Ён…ҚмҠӨнҠё (мӣҗмІң + obviation)

мӣҗмІң = CFP-2635 retro escalate_user нӣ„ліҙ A. PMO cross-Story pattern_count 2 (ADR-045 В§D-9 forcing function):

| CFP | мһҗкё°мЈјмһҘ(over-claim) | мӢӨм ң кІ°н•Ё | кІҖм¶ң lane | evidence (firsthand) |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| CFP-2635 | docstring "catastrophic backtracking 0" / "resource exhaustion л°©м–ҙ" / "per-file scan cap = DoS к°Җл“ң" | `_leading_token` slice-in-loop + per-line length лҜёbound = O(nВІ) (1.5MB лӢЁмқјлқјмқё >60s) | ліҙм•Ҳн…ҢмҠӨнҠё FIX SF-1 | `scripts/lib/check_shell_test_masking.py:30` (SF-1 м •м • м»Өл°Ӣ verbatim) |
| CFP-2591 | мЈјм„қ "nested quantifier 0" (ReDoS-safe мһҗм№ӯ) | `_RE_ALLOW_COUNTERFACTUAL` sequential unbounded `.*` 2м—°мҶҚ = quadratic backtracking (64KB=6.3s) | ліҙм•Ҳн…ҢмҠӨнҠё P2 ReDoS FIX | `git show 9c13ebbc` ("nested quantifier 0" мһҗм№ӯ м •м •, anti-theater) |

лҸ„л©”мқё ліём§Ҳ = **мһҗкё°м°ёмЎ° м •м§Ғ к°ӯ** вҖ” over-claim/false-coverage лҘј мһЎлҠ” dogfood governance tool мқҙ мһҗкё° docstring/мЈјм„қм—җм„ң лҸҷмў… over-claim мқ„ лӮҙкі , ліҙм•Ҳн…ҢмҠӨнҠё lane мқҙ write **нӣ„** лҠҰкІҢ catch(мўҢн–Ҙ мӢӨнҢЁ).

obviation (Story В§2.1 мҡ”кө¬мӮ¬н•ӯлҰ¬л·° 3-way CONFIRM): ethos(ADR-119 research-before-claims) = мЎ°мӮ¬ лІ”мң„ лӮҙ м»ӨлІ„(лӢЁ declarative-only + agent л°ңнҷ” м¶•, write-time docstring artifact м¶• лҜёлӘ…лӘ…) / detection(ліҙм•Ҳн…ҢмҠӨнҠё execution-backed probe) = мң нҡЁ(2/2 catch, лӢЁ мўҢн–Ҙ мӢӨнҢЁ) / ceiling(ADR-151 В§кІ°м •7) = мғҒмҶҚ SSOT. **мһ”м—¬ = write-time м •м§Ғ forcing л¶Җмһ¬(registry 0кұҙ)**. вҶ’ мӢ к·ң mechanism CLASS м•„лӢҢ **В§кІ°м • 15/В§кІ°м • 11 presence-lint нҢЁн„ҙмқҳ artifact-class нҷ•мһҘ**мңјлЎң м¶©лӢ№.

### В§B. В§кІ°м • 16 (мӢ м„Ө) вҖ” resource-safety-claim вҶ” proof-link write-time м •м§Ғ discipline

**Mandate**: governance/ліҙм•Ҳ tooling(evidence-check кІҢмқҙнҠёВ·ліҙм•Ҳ scriptВ·мӣҢнҒ¬н”ҢлЎң YAML)мқҳ **docstring + inline мЈјм„қ + ліҙм•Ҳ workflow YAML мЈјм„қ**м—җ resource-safety/ліөмһЎлҸ„/DoS-guard м•Ҳм „м„ұ-claim(closed-set: catastrophic backtracking 0 / ReDoS-safe / ReDoS-free / DoS к°Җл“ң / resource exhaustion л°©м–ҙ / scan cap = мҙқ мһ‘м—…лҹү bound / nested quantifier 0 / injection-safe м •м Ғ м•Ҳм „м„ұ лӢЁм • лҘҳ)мқ„ м“ё л•Ң, мһ‘м„ұ мЈјмІҙлҠ” (a) **paired proof-reference**(reproducer / wall-clock лІӨм№ҳл§ҲнҒ¬ / ліөмһЎлҸ„ нҡҢк·Җ self-test л§ҒнҒ¬) лҸҷл°ҳ, **лҳҗлҠ”** (b) **honest-ceiling**('bounded degradation, мһ„мқҳ мһ…л Ҙ л¬ҙн•ҙ м•„лӢҳ') downgrade лҘј мҲҳн–үн•ңлӢӨ. л¬ҙмҰқкұ° м•Ҳм „м„ұ лӢЁм • кёҲм§Җ.

**2-layer м°©м§Җ** (ADR-140 В§кІ°м •3 hybrid вҖ” dev declare вҶ’ review falsify):
- **Layer 1 (н–үмң„ mandate, AC-1a declared)**: write-time declaration mandate вҖ” roster/skill prose(мһ‘м„ұ мЈјмІҙ = SecurityArchitectAgent / DeveloperAgent / QADeveloperAgent / InfraEngineerAgent). н–үмң„(м •м§Ғн•ҳкІҢ м“°лҠ”к°Җ)лҠ” **м •м Ғ кі„мёЎ л¶Ҳк°Җ** вҶ’ declaration + лҰ¬л·°(м„Өкі„/кө¬нҳ„/ліҙм•Ҳ) falsify.
- **Layer 2 (artifact presence lint, AC-1b normative warning-tier)**: presence lint 5-piece chain мқҙ м•Ҳм „м„ұ-claim вҶ” paired proof-ref/ceiling мқҳ **presence** лҘј м •м Ғ кІҖмӮ¬. claim к°җм§Җ + proof-ref/ceiling л‘ҳ лӢӨ л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ FLAG.

**mechanism = В§кІ°м • 15/В§кІ°м • 11 presence-lint лӢөмҠө** (мӢ к·ң CLASS м•„лӢҳ):
- claim кІҖм¶ң: **affirmative-context closed-set л§Өм№ӯ** вҖ” `check-tier-honesty.py:8-9,57-58`(кёҚм • enforcement нҶ нҒ° closed-set л§Ң л§Өм№ӯ, м •м§Ғн•ң л¶Җм • м„ңмҲ  лҜёл§Өм№ӯ, лӢЁмҲң grep кёҲм§Җ) кё°лІ• лӢөмҠө. denial('... м•„лӢҳ')В·м •мқҳл¶Җ мһҗкё°м—ҙкұ°В·м •мұ… м—ҙкұ° л¬ёл§Ҙ EXEMPT.
- evidence presence: лҸҷмқј нҢҢмқј claim-adjacent scan вҶ’ proof-ref closed-set OR ceiling closed-set presence. `check_issue_body_claim_pre_screen.py:51,54,70`(PER_FILE_SCAN_CAP + ANNOTATION_MARKER м •м Ғ substring + code-span/fenced/blockquote EXEMPT guard) кө¬мЎ° лӢөмҠө.
- grandfather: `docs/resource-safety-claim-baseline.yaml` new-only subtract(legacy 27-file лҸҷкІ° вҖ” `deferred-followup-baseline.yaml` нҳ•нӢҖ). мӢ к·ң over-claim л§Ң surface.

**honesty-ceiling(ADR-151 В§кІ°м •7 мғҒмҶҚ, verify вҠӢ presence disjoint)**: lint мқҖ proof-ref/ceiling **presence** л§Ң кІҖмӮ¬ вҖ” claim **м°ёлҗЁ** лҜёк°•м ң(claim-without-any-proof-link л§Ң мўҢн–Ҙ л…ём¶ң, л¶Ҳмҷ„м „ proof лҠ” PASS). "over-claim мҷ„м „ лҙүмқё" hard-claim кёҲм§Җ.

**5-piece chain** (Phase 2 mechanical wire, CFP-2635 ADR-060 Amd 22 лҸҷнҳ•):
1. Python SSOT `scripts/lib/check_resource_safety_claim_proof.py`
2. thin wrapper `scripts/check-resource-safety-claim-proof.sh` (ADR-061 В§кІ°м •1 python3 exec forward)
3. byte-identical workflow pair `{templates/github-workflows,.github/workflows}/resource-safety-claim-proof-presence.yml` (ADR-005 sha256, `on: pull_request`[NOT pull_request_target] + `permissions: contents:read`(+pull-requests:write comment) + `runs-on: ${{ fromJSON(vars.CI_RUNS_ON_LINUX_JSON || '["ubuntu-latest"]') }}` self-hosted, injection-safe env-only)
4. discriminating self-test `tests/scripts/test_check-resource-safety-claim-proof.sh`
5. registry warning-tier entry `resource-safety-claim-proof-presence` + `hotfix-bypass:resource-safety-claim-proof-presence`(label-registry MINOR)

### В§C. вҳ… мһҗкё°м°ёмЎ° DoS нҡҢн”ј (л©”нғҖ-мһ¬к·Җ вҖ” CFP-2635 O(nВІ) көҗнӣҲ н•„мҲҳ л°ҳмҳҒ)

ліё lint лҸ„ нҢҢмқј лӮҙмҡ©мқ„ regex мҠӨмә”н•ңлӢӨ = **CFP-2635 SF-1 кіј лҸҷмқј н‘ңл©ҙ**. CFP-2635 лҠ” мң„нҳ‘ м¶• enumeration м—җм„ң **algorithmic-complexity м¶•(T-2) + line-length м¶•(T-3) мқ„ лҲ„лқҪ**н•ҙ O(nВІ) DoS лҘј н’Ҳм—ҲлӢӨ. ліё В§кІ°м • 16 lint мқҖ 4-axis bound лҘј **мІҳмқҢл¶Җн„°**(мӮ¬нӣ„ м •м • м•„лӢҢ born-safe) л°°м„ н•ңлӢӨ:

| м¶• | мң„нҳ‘ | мҷ„нҷ” (born-safe) |
|---|---|---|
| T-1 regex backtracking | nested quantifier catastrophic backtracking | м „ regex anchored + bounded quantifier, **nested quantifier 0**, closed-set лҰ¬н„°лҹҙ substring мҡ°м„  |
| **T-2 algorithmic-complexity** (вҳ… CFP-2635 лҲ„лқҪ) | slice-in-loop `t = t[m.end():]` = O(nВІ) | **index-advance O(n)** tokenize (`re.match(t, pos)` offset м „м§„, slice мһ¬ліөмӮ¬ 0) вҖ” `check_shell_test_masking.py:235-252` / `check_spawn_prompt_fact_verify.py` лӢөмҠө. claim-adjacent scan window bounded |
| **T-3 line-length** (вҳ… CFP-2635 лҲ„лқҪ, count-cap лі„к°ң м¶•) | arbitrary кёёмқҙ лӢЁмқјлқјмқё(1.5MB) вҶ’ лқјмқё-кёёмқҙ мқҳмЎҙ кІҪлЎң мҙқ мһ‘м—…лҹү лҜёbound | **`MAX_PHYSICAL_LINE_LEN` per-physical-line truncate-scan** вҖ” `PER_FILE_SCAN_CAP` count-cap кіј **лі„к°ң м¶•**. CFP-2635 SF-1 мқҙ м •нҷ•нһҲ мқҙ м¶• л¶Җмһ¬лЎң O(nВІ) |
| T-4 read-path | лі‘лҰ¬м Ғ лӢӨн–ү нҢҢмқј unbounded read | `itertools.islice(f, PER_FILE_SCAN_CAP)` лқјмқё count bound. мҙқ мһ‘м—…лҹү вүӨ cap Г— line-len мң н•ң bound |

**мһҗкё° docstring м •м§Ғ**: ліё lint мқҳ docstring/мЈјм„қмқҖ мһҗкё° resource-safety лҘј over-claim н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ вҖ” мҷ„нҷ”лҠ” CPU/л©”лӘЁлҰ¬ мҙқ мһ‘м—…лҹү bound мқҙм§Җ "мһ„мқҳ мһ…л Ҙ л¬ҙн•ҙ" к°Җ м•„лӢҳ(bounded degradation, `check_shell_test_masking.py:39` мғҒмҶҚ). "catastrophic backtracking 0" м„ңмҲ  мҳҶм—җ proof-reference(self-test ReDoS/O(nВІ) нҡҢк·Җк°Җл“ң test кІҪлЎң) лҸҷл°ҳ вҶ’ **мқҙ lint мқҳ docstring мһҗмІҙк°Җ мһҗкё° lint мқ„ нҶөкіј**(AC-3 self-application).

### В§D. A2-5 нҢҗм • вҖ” мӢ к·ң ADR м•„лӢҳ (ADR-082 Amendment м •н•©)

- ADR-082 = write-time self-write verify super-class(ліём§Ҳ м„ м–ё `:676` "мһ‘м„ұн•ң к°’ мһҗмІҙк°Җ мӮ¬мӢӨкіј мқјм№ҳн•ҳлҠ”к°Җ verify нӣ„ write").
- **В§кІ°м • 11** мқҙ мқҙлҜё super-class лҘј **code-level artifact write-time**(test binding / script error visibility)лЎң нҷ•мһҘ вҖ” мҪ”л“ң artifact write-time discipline м„ лЎҖ.
- **В§кІ°м • 15** к°Җ мқҙлҜё **claim closed-set вҶ’ paired annotation presence lint**(issue-body-claim-pre-screen) mechanism нҷ•лҰҪ вҖ” presence-lint carrier.
- disjoint м¶• мҡ°л Ө(verify вҠӢ presence) лҠ” **ADR-082 м•Ҳм—җм„ң мқҙлҜё н•ҙмҶҢ** вҖ” кё°мЎҙ carrier(issue-body / spawn-prompt-fact-verify)лҸ„ presence-lint(full verify м•„лӢҳ)мқҙл©° presence = verify мқҳ honesty-ceiling кё°кі„ floor. вҶ’ ліё В§кІ°м • 16 = **3лІҲм§ё sibling presence-lint carrier**(мғҲ claim class = resource-safety/DoS-guard, мғҲ artifact class = docstring/мЈјм„қ/workflow YAML) + ADR-151 ceiling лӘ…мӢң мғҒмҶҚ = **мӢ к·ң mechanism CLASS м•„лӢҳ вҶ’ Amendment м •н•©**(мӢ к·ң ADR = over-fragmentation).
- нқЎмҲҳ кё°к°Ғ лҢҖм•Ҳ: ADR-119 В§кІ°м • specialize(declarative-only + л°ңнҷ” м¶• вҶ’ artifact м¶• лҜёлӘ…лӘ…) / ADR-140 amendment(subject = лҰ¬нҢ©н„°л§Ғ hygiene disjoint, мһҗкё°лӘЁмҲң кё°к°Ғ м„ лЎҖ лҸҷнҳ•) / ADR-151 AC-7 нҷ•мһҘ(execution-liveness вҠҘ docstring-claim disjoint, мғҒмҶҚл§Ң) вҖ” 3 лҢҖм•Ҳ лӘЁл‘җ subject/axis disjoint вҶ’ кё°к°Ғ. **ADR-082 = мөңк·јм ‘ home**.
- atomic claim: мӢ к·ң ADR м•„лӢҲлҜҖлЎң ADR-number OCC л¶Ҳмҡ”. Amendment 38 = id ascending(max=37 firsthand вҶ’ next=38). Orchestrator commit-time max+1 мһ¬кІҖмҰқ мқҳл¬ҙ(лі‘л ¬м„ём…ҳ reslot лҢҖл№„, META-self-application В§кІ°м • 10.D кҙҖлЎҖ).

### В§E. Wave split (Phase 1 / Phase 2)

- **Phase 1 PR** (internal-docs #1908): ліё Amendment(ADR-082 В§кІ°м • 16) + write-time mandate roster/skill prose(Layer 1) + registry declarative anchor(`mechanical_enforcement_actions[]` resource-safety-claim-proof-presence status flip) + change-plan(`wrapper/change-plans/cfp-2646-resource-safety-claim-proof-lint.md`) + Story В§3/В§7 + named carrier declare.
- **Phase 2 PR**: 5-piece mechanical wire(Layer 2 lint + self-test + workflow + grandfather baseline) + registry status Active + label-registry MINOR + plugin.json MINOR(мӢ к·ң evidence-check capability).
- tier = warning(ADR-060 В§кІ°м •5, continue-on-error, PR merge л¬ҙм°ЁлӢЁ). **blocking мҠ№кІ©**(FP мӢӨмёЎ = ADR-060 evidence-gate нҶөкіј нӣ„) + м •мұ…л¬ём„ң н‘ңл©ҙ over-claim sweep + consumer м „нҢҢ = **лі„лҸ„ named carrier**(`CFP-TBD` кёҲм§Җ вҖ” deferral-carrier-declared no-TBD lint лҢҖмғҒ).
